\subsubsection[The Westminster Confession of Faith of 1647]{{The Westminster Confession of
Faith}

\index{Faith:saving ``f10!}

\section{Chapter 1 -- Of the Holy Scripture} \index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}1.1\ \ Although the light of nature and the works of creation\index{God's  attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} do so far manifest the\index{Providence:manifests goodness of God ``f10!} goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!}, wisdom, and power\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!} of God, as to leave men unexcusable\index{Unbelievers:unexcusable ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:19-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:32\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  32, pg. ``f30!} with Romans 2:1.} yet are they not sufficient to\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:sufficient for that time ``f10!} give that knowledge of God\index{Revelation:natural:not sufficient knowledge of God ``f10!} and of His will, which is necessary unto salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} Therefore it pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} the Lord, at sundry times, and in divers manners\index{Revelation:sundry times and divers manners ``f10!}, to reveal Himself, and to declare that\index{Revelation:special declaration ``f10!} His will unto His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and afterwards, for the better preserving\index{Church:to preserve truth ``f10!} and propagating\index{Scripture:for propagating truth ``f10!} of the truth, and\index{Oaths and Vows:assertion of truth ``f10!} for the more sure establishment\index{Scripture:for establishment and comfort of Church ``f10!} and comfort of the Church against\index{Church:institution ``f10!} the corruption of the\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:flesh ``f10!} flesh, and the\index{flesh, sinful nature ``f10!} malice of\index{Satan:malice of ``f10!} Satan and of\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} the world, to commit the same wholly unto writing:\index{Scripture:written ``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs 22:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  22, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9-21\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  22, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:3-4\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 7, 10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, 7, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 8:19-20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.} which makes the Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} to be most necessary;\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} those former ways of God's revealing His\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!} will unto His people being now ceased\index{Scripture:other forms of revelation have ceased ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.2\ \ Under the name of Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}, or the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!} written, are now contained all the books of the Old and New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, which are these\index{Scripture:Old and New Testaments ``f10!}:  
\bigskip
{\centering \textit{Of the Old Testament}\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}\textit{:} \par}  \begin{multicols}{3} Genesis  Exodus  Leviticus  Numbers  Deuteronomy  Joshua  Judges  Ruth  1 Samuel  2 Samuel  1 Kings  2 Kings  1 Chronicles  2 Chronicles  Ezra  Nehemiah  Esther  Job  Psalms  Proverbs  Ecclesiastes  Song of Songs  Isaiah  Jeremiah  Lamentations  Ezekiel  Daniel  Hosea  Joel  Amos  Obadiah  Jonah  Micah  Nahum  Habakkuk  Zephaniah  Haggai  Zechariah  Malachi  \end{multicols}  
\bigskip
{\centering \textit{Of the New Testament}\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}\textit{:} \par} \begin{multicols}{3} Matthew  Mark  Luke  John  Acts  Romans  1 Corinthians  2 Corinthians  Galatians  Ephesians  Philippians  Colossians  1 Thessalonians  2 Thessalonians  1 Timothy  2 Timothy  Titus  Philemon  Hebrews  James  1 Peter  2 Peter  1 John  2 John  3 John  Jude  Revelation \end{multicols}  
\bigskip
All which are given by inspiration of\index{Scripture:inspired by God ``f10!} God, to be the rule of faith\index{Faith:rule of ``f10!} and life.\footnote{\ Luke 16:29, 31\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  29, 31, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:18-19\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
1.3\ \ The books commonly called Apocrypha\index{Apocrypha:not God breathed ``f10!}, not being of divine inspiration, are no part of the canon\index{Scripture:canon ``f10!} of the Scripture; and\index{Scripture:Apocrypha not part of canon ``f10!} therefore are of no authority in the Church of God\index{Church:God's ``f10!}, nor to be any otherwise approved, or made use of, than other human writings\index{Apocrypha:human writings ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 24:27, 44\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  27, 44, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
1.4\ \ The authority of the Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}, for which it ought to be believed and\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} obeyed\index{Scripture:to be:obeyed:because word of God ``f10!}, depends not upon the testimony\index{Scripture:authority not from testimony of any man ``f10!} of any man, or Church\index{Church:institution ``f10!}; but wholly upon God (who is truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!} itself) the author thereof\index{Scripture:authored by God ``f10!}: and therefore it is to be received because it is the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}, 21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, 21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.5\ \ We may be moved and induced by the testimony\index{Scripture:testimony of the Church ``f10!} of the Church to\index{Church:institution ``f10!} a high and reverent\index{Scripture:to be:treated with reverent esteem ``f10!} esteem of the\index{Scripture:to be:esteemed ``f10!} Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 3:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} And the heavenliness\index{Scripture:heavenly matter ``f10!} of the matter, the efficacy\index{Scripture:efficacy of doctrine ``f10!} of the doctrine, the\index{Doctrine:of Scripture ``f10!} majesty of the\index{Scripture:majesty of the style ``f10!} style, the consent of all\index{Scripture:consent of all parts ``f10!} the parts, the scope of the whole (which is, to give all glory\index{Scripture:gives glory to God ``f10!} to God), the full discovery\index{Scripture:makes full discovery of the only way of salvation ``f10!} it makes of the only way of man's salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, the many other incomparable excellencies\index{Scripture:excellency ``f10!}, and the entire perfection thereof\index{Scripture:perfection of ``f10!}, are arguments whereby it does abundantly evidence itself to be the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}: yet notwithstanding, our full persuasion\index{Scripture:Holy Spirit persuades us that it is word of God ``f10!} and assurance of the\index{Assurance:that God's word is true ``f10!} infallible truth\index{Scripture:infallible truth ``f10!} and divine authority\index{Scripture:divine authority ``f10!} thereof, is from the inward\index{Scripture:witnessed inwardly by Holy Spirit ``f10!} work of the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} bearing witness by\index{Scripture:witness to heart of man ``f10!} and with the Word in our hearts\index{Heart:new:through ministry of Word ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 2:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0, 27\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  20, 27, pg. ``f30!}; John 16:13-14\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:10, 11-12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  10, 11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
1.6\ \ The whole counsel of God\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} concerning all things necessary for His own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, man's salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, faith, and life, is either expressly set\index{Scripture:interpretation:some things expressly set down ``f10!} down in Scripture, or by good and necessary consequence\index{Scripture:interpretation:deduced by good and necessary consequence ``f10!} may be deduced from Scripture: unto which nothing at any time is to be added, whether by new revelations\index{Revelation:new, not added to Scripture ``f10!} of the Spirit, or\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit ``f10!} traditions\index{Scripture:supersedes traditions of men ``f10!} of men.\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 1:8-9\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:2\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} Nevertheless we acknowledge the inward illumination\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:provides inner illumination ``f10!} of the Spirit of God\index{Holy Spirit:God's Spirit ``f10!} to be necessary for the saving understanding\index{Salvation:by working of Holy Spirit ``f10!} of such things as are revealed in the Word:\index{Scripture:word of God:standard for:life ``f10!}\footnote{\ John 6:45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  45, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:9-12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   9-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and that there are some circumstances\index{Worship:circumstances ``f10!} concerning the worship of God, and\index{Worship:correct:instituted by God ``f10!} government of\index{Church government:government ``f10!} the Church, common\index{Church:institution ``f10!} to human actions and societies\index{Scripture:interpretation:circumstances of societies ``f10!}, which are to be ordered\index{Scripture:interpretation:by light of nature according rules of Word ``f10!} by the light of nature and Christian prudence, according\index{Scripture:interpretation:by prudence according rules of Word ``f10!} to the general rules of the Word, which are always to be observed\index{Scripture:interpretation:general rules to be observed ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:13-14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 14:26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}, 40\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  26, 40, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.7\ \ All things in Scripture are not alike plain in\index{Scripture:not all parts plain in themselves ``f10!} themselves, nor alike clear unto all:\footnote{\ 2 Peter 3:16\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} yet those things which are necessary to be known, believed, and\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} observed for salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, are so clearly propounded\index{Scripture:what necessary to know, clearly propounded ``f10!} and opened in some place of Scripture or\index{Scripture:interpretation:scripture with scripture ``f10!} other, that not only the learned\index{Scripture:useful for learned and unlearned ``f10!}, but the unlearned, in a due use of the ordinary means, may\index{Scripture:understandable:through ordinary means ``f10!} attain unto a sufficient\index{Scripture:understandable:by unlearned ``f10!} understanding of them.\footnote{\ Psalm 119:105\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 105, pg. ``f30!}, 130\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 105, 130, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.8\ \ The Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!} in Hebrew\index{Scripture:Old Testament Hebrew ``f10!} (which was the native language of the people of God of old), and the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!} in Greek\index{Scripture:New Testament Greek ``f10!} (which, at the time of the writing of\index{Scripture:written ``f10!} it was most generally known to the nations\index{Scripture:written in languages known to nations ``f10!}), being immediately inspired\index{Scripture:inspired by God ``f10!} by God, and, by His singular care and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} kept pure in\index{Scripture:kept pure in all ages ``f10!} all ages, are therefore authentical\index{Scripture:original language:versions authentic ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 5:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} so as, in all controversies\index{Scripture:determine all controversies ``f10!} of religion, the Church is\index{Church:institution ``f10!} finally to appeal unto them.\footnote{\ Isaiah 8:20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!} ,Acts 15:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, 46, pg. ``f30!}.} But, because these original tongues\index{Scripture:original language:not known to all ``f10!} are not known to all the people of God, who have right unto, and interest in the\index{Scripture:all people have interest (share) in ``f10!} Scriptures, and are commanded, in the\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!} fear of\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!} God, to read and search the\index{Heart:God alone able to search ``f10!}m\index{Scripture:to be:searched ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} therefore they are to be translated\index{Scripture:to be:translated into common (vulgar) languages ``f10!} into the vulgar language of every nation unto which they come,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:6, 9, 11-12, 24, 27-28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.   6, 9, 11-12, 24, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} that the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!} dwelling plentifully in all, they may worship Him\index{Worship:acceptable manner ``f10!} in an acceptable manner;\footnote{\ Colossians 3:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and, through patience and comfort of the Scriptures\index{Scripture:comforts and builds up believers ``f10!}, may have hope\index{Scripture:provides hope ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.9\ \ The infallible\index{Scripture:interpretation:scripture with scripture ``f10!} rule of interpretation of Scripture is the Scripture itself: and therefore, when there is a question about the true and full sense of any Scripture (which is not manifold, but\index{Scripture:interpretation:not manifold, but on sense ``f10!} one), it must be searched\index{Scripture:to be:searched ``f10!} and known by other places that speak more clearly.\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0-21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}  
\bigskip
1.10\ \ The supreme judge by\index{Scripture:supreme judge of controversies ``f10!} which all controversies\index{Scripture:determine all controversies ``f10!} of religion are to be determined, and all decrees\index{Church councils:decrees ``f10!} of councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}, opinions of\index{Scripture:final authority, not opinions of ancient writers ``f10!} ancient writers, doctrines\index{Doctrine:false:of men ``f10!} of men, and private spirits, are to be examined\index{Scripture:to be:used to examine all doctrines ``f10!}; and in whose sentence we are to rest; can be no other but the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} speaking in the Scripture\index{Scripture:word of God:Holy Spirit speaking ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:29, 31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  29, 31, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!} with Acts 28:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  28, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 2 -- Of God, and of the Holy Trinity} \index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!} 2.1\ \ There is but one only,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 8:4, 6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   4, 6, pg. ``f30!}.} living, and true God:\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 1:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 10:10\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} who is infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:knowledge ``f10!} in being and perfection\index{God's attributes:perfect blessedness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Job 11:7-9\index{18 Job:ch.  11, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Job 26:14\index{18 Job:ch.  26, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} a most pure\index{God's attributes:a spirit, most pure ``f10!} spirit,\footnote{\ John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} invisible,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} without body, parts,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:15-16\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!} with Luke 24:39\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} or passions\index{God's attributes:no passions ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 14:11, 15\index{44 Acts:ch.  14, v.  11, 15, pg. ``f30!}.} immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 1:17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Malachi 3:6\index{39 Malachi:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} immense\index{God's attributes:immense ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Kings 8:27\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 23:23-24\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  23, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} eternal,\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 90:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  90, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} incomprehensible\index{God's attributes:incomprehensible ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 145:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} almighty\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 17:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 4:8\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!},\footnote{\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!} most holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most ``f10!},\footnote{\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}\index{19 Psalms:ch. 115, v.   3, pg. ``f30!} most absolute\index{God's attributes:absolute ``f10!},\footnote{\index{02 Exodus:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!} things according to the counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own immutable and most righteous will\index{God's attributes:righteousness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} for His own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!};\footnote{\ Proverbs 16:4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  16, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} most loving\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 4:8, 16\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.   8, 16, pg. ``f30!}.} gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}, merciful\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!}, long-suffering\index{God's attributes:long-suffering ``f10!}, abundant in goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!} and truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!}, forgiving iniquity\index{God's attributes:forgiving iniquity ``f10!}, transgression, and\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} sin;\footnote{\ Exodus 34:6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} the rewarder\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!} of them that diligently seek\index{Salvation:for those who diligently seek God ``f10!} Him;\footnote{\ Hebrews 11:6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and withal, most just and terrible\index{Judgement:just and terrible ``f10!} in His judgments\index{God's attributes:judge ``f10!},\footnote{\ Nehemiah 9:32-33\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.  32-33, pg. ``f30!}.} hating\index{God's attributes:hates sin ``f10!} all sin,\footnote{\ Psalm 5:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.   5, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} and who will by no means clear the guilty\index{guilt ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Nahum 1:2-3\index{34 Nahum:ch.   1, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 34:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}     
\bigskip
2.2\ \ God has all life\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 5:26\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} glory,\footnote{\ Acts 7:2\index{44 Acts:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 119:68\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  68, pg. ``f30!}.} blessedness,\index{God's attributes:perfect blessedness ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} in and of Himself; and is alone in and unto Himself all-sufficient\index{God's attributes:all-sufficient ``f10!}, not standing in need of any creatures\index{creatures ``f10!} which He has made,\footnote{\ Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} nor deriving\index{God's attributes:glory:not derived from creatures ``f10!} any glory from them,\footnote{\ Job 22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} but only manifesting\index{God's attributes:glory:manifested ``f10!} His own glory in, by, unto, and upon them: He is the alone fountain\index{God's attributes:creator:fountain of existence ``f10!} of all being, of whom, through whom, and to whom are all things;\footnote{\ Rom 11:36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} and has most sovereign\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} dominion over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!}m\index{God's attributes:sovereign dominion ``f10!}, to do by them, for them, or upon them whatsoever Himself pleases\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Revelation 4:11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 4:25, 35\index{27 Daniel:ch.   4, v.  25, 35, pg. ``f30!}.} In His sight all things are open and manifest;\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} His knowledge\index{God's attributes:omniscience ``f10!} is infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:knowledge ``f10!}, infallible, and\index{God's attributes:infallible fore-knowledge ``f10!} independent\index{God's attributes:knowledge independent of creature ``f10!} upon the creature,\footnote{\ Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 147:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 147, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} so as nothing is to Him contingent\index{Causation:no contingency with God ``f10!}, or uncertain.\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 11:5\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  11, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} He is most holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most ``f10!} in all His counsels\index{God's attributes:holy:counsels ``f10!}, in all His works\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!}, and in all His commands\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 145:17\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:12\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} To Him is due from angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men, and every other creature, whatsoever worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}, service, or obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} He is pleased to require of them.\footnote{\ Revelation 5:12-14\index{66 Revelation:ch.   5, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.}     
\bigskip
2.3\ \ In the unity\index{God's attributes:unity of persons ``f10!} of the Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!} there be three persons\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!}, of one substance\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!}, power, and eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}; God the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, God the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and God the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 5:7\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:16-17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} The Father is of none, neither begotten\index{Holy Spirit:not begotten ``f10!}, nor proceeding: the\index{Father:God the, no procession ``f10!} Son is eternally\index{Jesus:begotten eternally ``f10!} begotten of the\index{Jesus:begotten by the Father ``f10!} Father:\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} the Holy Ghost eternally proceeding from\index{Holy Spirit:procession from Father and Son ``f10!} the Father and the Son.\footnote{\ John 15:26\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
  

\section{Chapter 3 -- Of God's Eternal Decree} \index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}3.1\ \ God from all eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!} did, by the most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will, freely, and unchangeably ordain whatsoever\index{Predestination:all that happens ``f10!} comes to pass:\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  15, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} yet so, as thereby neither is God the author\index{Sin:God not author or approver of ``f10!} of sin,\footnote{\ James 1:13, 17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  13, 17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:5\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} nor is violence\index{Causation:will of creatures:not destroyed by predestination ``f10!} offered to the will of the creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, nor is the liberty or\index{Liberty:natural ``f10!} contingency\index{Causation:contingency ``f10!} of second causes\index{Causation:second causes ``f10!} taken away, but rather established.\footnote{\ Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 17:12\index{40 Matthew:ch.  17, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:27-28\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; John 19:11\index{43 John:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 16:33\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  16, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.2\ \ Although God knows whatsoever\index{God's attributes:omniscience ``f10!} may or can come to pass upon all supposed conditions\index{Predestination:not conditional ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 23:11-12\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  23, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 11:21, 23\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet has He not decreed\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} anything because He foresaw\index{Predestination:not based on God's foresight:of events ``f10!} it as future, or as that which would come to pass upon such conditions.\footnote{\ Romans 9:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}, 13, 16\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, 13, 16, pg. ``f30!}, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, 13, 16, 18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.3\ \ By the decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of God, for the manifestation of His glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, some men and angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:21\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}.} are predestinated\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!} unto everlasting life\index{everlasting life ``f10!}, and others fore-ordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!} to everlasting death\index{Death:everlasting ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 9:22, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  22, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 16:4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  16, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.4\ \ These angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men, thus predestinated\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!}, and fore-ordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!}, are particularly and unchangeably designed\index{Angels:unchangeably designed ``f10!}, and their number so certain and definite\index{Angels:definite number, no increase or decrease ``f10!}, that it cannot be either increased or diminished.\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 2:19\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; John 13:18\index{43 John:ch.  13, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.5\ \ Those of mankind\index{Predestination:mankind:unto life ``f10!} that are predestinated\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!} unto life, God, before the foundation\index{Predestination:before foundation of world. ``f10!} of the world was laid, according to His eternal and immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} purpose, and the secret counsel and\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} good pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} of His will, has chosen\index{Election:chosen by God ``f10!}, in Christ, unto everlasting glory,\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:everlasting ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, 9, pg. ``f30!}, 11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, 9, 11, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 1:9\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 5:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} out of His mere free grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} and love, without\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!} any foresight\index{Predestination:not based on God's foresight:of faith ``f10!} of faith or good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!}, or perseverance\index{Good works:not foreseen by God as cause of election ``f10!} in either of them, or any other thing in the creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, as conditions\index{Predestination:not conditional ``f10!}, or causes moving Him thereunto:\footnote{\ Romans 9:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}, 13, 16\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, 13, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, 9, pg. ``f30!}.} and all to the praise of His\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} glorious grace\index{Grace:glorious ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, 12, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.6.\ \ As God has appointed the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} unto glory\index{Believers:elected unto glory ``f10!}, so has He, by the eternal and most\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} free purpose of His will, fore-ordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!} all the means thereunto.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 1:2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} Wherefore they who are elected\index{Election:chosen by God ``f10!}, being fallen in\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} Adam, are\index{Adam:guilt of first sin on all mankind ``f10!} redeemed\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!} by Christ,\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 5:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and kept by His power\index{Perseverance:kept by God's power ``f10!} through faith, unto salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 1:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} Neither are any other redeemed by Christ, effectually called, justified, adopted, sanctified, and saved, but\index{Salvation:only the elect ``f10!} the elect only.\footnote{\ John 17:9\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip
3.7\ \ The rest of mankind\index{Predestination:mankind:unto reprobation ``f10!} God was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}, according to the unsearchable\index{Providence:unsearchable wise counsel ``f10!} counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will, whereby He extends or withholds\index{Providence:God withholds mercy, grace, favour as he wills ``f10!} mercy, as\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} He pleases, for the glory of His\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} sovereign\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} power over His creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, to pass by; and to ordain the\index{Predestination:Jesus as mediator ``f10!}m\index{Predestination:unto wrath ``f10!} to dishonour\index{Resurrection:wicked raised in dishonour ``f10!} and wrath, for\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!} their sin, to the praise of His\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} glorious justice\index{God's attributes:administers justice ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 11:25-26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:17\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}, 18, 21-22\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  17, 18, 21-22, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 2:19\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 4\index{65 Jude:v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:8\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
3.8\ \ The doctrine of this\index{Doctrine:of predestination ``f10!} high mystery\index{Predestination:mystery of ``f10!} of predestination\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!} is to be handled with special prudence and\index{Predestination:doctrine to be handled with prudence ``f10!} care,\footnote{{\ Romans 9:20}\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  29, v.  29, pg. ``f30!} that men attending the will of God revealed in His Word, and\index{Scripture:word of God:standard for:life ``f10!} yielding\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} obedience thereunto, may, from the certainty of their effectual vocation\index{Redemption:effectually:assured ``f10!}, be assured of\index{Assurance:of election ``f10!} their eternal election.\index{Election:eternal ``f10!}\footnote{\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, reverence, and admiration\index{Predestination:to elicit admiration of God ``f10!} of God,\footnote{\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}, diligence, and abundant consolation to\index{Predestination:consolation for believers ``f10!} all that sincerely obey\index{Gospel:to be sincerely obeyed ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 11:5-6, 20\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.   5-6, 20, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 10:20\index{42 Luke:ch.  10, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 4 -- Of Creation} 4.1\ \ It pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} God the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:2-3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Job 26:13\index{18 Job:ch.  26, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Job 33:4\index{18 Job:ch.  33, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} for the manifestation of the glory of His\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} eternal power\index{God's attributes:eternal power ``f10!}, wisdom, and goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 10:12\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 104:24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 33:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} in the beginning, to create, or\index{God's attributes:creator:from nothing ``f10!} make of nothing, the world, and all things therein whether visible or\index{God's attributes:creator:of visible or invisible ``f10!} invisible, in\index{Creation:visible and invisible ``f10!} the space of six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days; and all very good.\footnote{\ Genesis 1 chap. Hebrews 11:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the }\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription }}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Clarifications}}\textcolor{black}{).}}   
\bigskip
4.2\ \ After God\index{Mankind:created:attributes ``f10!} had made all other creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, He created man\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!}, male\index{Mankind:male and female ``f10!} and female\index{Mankind:created:male and female ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} with reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!} and immortal\index{Mankind:immortal soul ``f10!} souls,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!} with Ecclesiastes 12:7\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!} \& Luke 23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  43, pg. ``f30!} and Matthew 10:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} endued with knowledge\index{Mankind:created:with knowledge, righteousness, and holiness ``f10!}, righteousness, and true holiness\index{Mankind:created:holy ``f10!}, after His own image\index{Mankind:image of God ``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:10\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} having the law of God written in their hearts\index{God's law:written on man's heart ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} and power to fulfil it\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} and yet under a possibility of transgressing\index{Mankind:created:with possibility of transgressing ``f10!}, being left to the liberty of their\index{Liberty:of own will ``f10!} own will, which was subject unto change.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} Beside this law written in their hearts, they received a command, not\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!} to eat of the tree of the\index{Tree:of the knowledge of good and evil ``f10!} knowledge of good and evil, which while they kept, they were happy\index{happiness ``f10!} in their communion with God\index{Communion:with God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-11, 23\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   8-11, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} and had dominion over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!} creatures.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, 28, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 5 -- Of Providence} \index{Providence:providence ``f10!}5.1\ \ God the great Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things ``f10!} of all things does uphold\index{Providence:upholds all creatures ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} direct, dispose, and\index{Providence:God disposes all things for his glory ``f10!} govern\index{Providence:governing all ``f10!} all creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, actions, and things,\footnote{\ Daniel 4:34-35\index{27 Daniel:ch.   4, v.  34-35, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 135:6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 135, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26, 28\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25-26, 28, pg. ``f30!}; Job 38 to 41 chapters.} from the greatest even to the least,\footnote{\ Matthew 10:29, 30-31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  10, v.  29, 30-31, pg. ``f30!}.} by His most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 15:3\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  15, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 104:24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 145:17\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} according to His infallible\index{God's attributes:infallible fore-knowledge ``f10!} fore-knowledge\index{God's attributes:foreknowledge ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 94:8, 11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  94, v.   8, 11, pg. ``f30!}.} and the free and immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will,\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 33:10-11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} to the praise of the\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} glory of His\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} wisdom, power\index{God's attributes:listed (definition of God) ``f10!}, justice, goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!}, and mercy.\footnote{\ Isaiah 63:14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  63, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:10\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:17\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 45:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 145:7\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
5.2\ \ Although, in relation to the\index{Causation:relation to fore-knowledge ``f10!} fore-knowledge\index{God's attributes:foreknowledge ``f10!} and decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of God, the first Cause\index{Causation:first cause ``f10!}, all things come to pass immutably\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!}, and infallibly\index{Providence:infallible ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet, by the same providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, He orders them to fall out, according to the nature of second causes\index{Causation:second causes ``f10!}, either necessarily, freely, or\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} contingently\index{Causation:no contingency with God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 8:22\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}5\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 21:13\index{02 Exodus:ch.  21, v.  13, pg. ``f30!} with Deuteronomy 19:5\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  19, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 22:28, 34\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  22, v.  28, 34, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 10:6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
5.3\ \ God in His ordinary\index{Providence:ordinary means not binding on God ``f10!} providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} makes use of means,\footnote{\ Acts 27:31, 44\index{44 Acts:ch.  27, v.  31, 44, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 55:1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0-11\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Hosea 2:21-22\index{28 Hosea:ch.   2, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} yet is free to work without,\footnote{\ Hosea 1:7\index{28 Hosea:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Job 34:20\index{18 Job:ch.  34, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} above,\footnote{\ Romans 4:19-21\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}.} and against them at His pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Kings 6:6\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 3:27\index{27 Daniel:ch.   3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
5.4\ \ The almighty\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!} power, unsearchable\index{Providence:unsearchable wise counsel ``f10!} wisdom, and infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:goodness ``f10!} goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!} of God so far manifest themselves in\index{Providence:manifests goodness of God ``f10!} His providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, that it extends itself\index{Providence:extends even to first sin ``f10!} even to the first fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, and all other sins of angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men;\footnote{\ Romans 11:32\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32-34, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 24:1\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  24, v.   1, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Chronicles 21:1\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  21, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 22:22-23\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  22, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Chronicles 10:4, 13-14\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  10, v.   4, 13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 16:10\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  16, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:27-28\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} and that not by a bare permission\index{Sin:God purposes and permits for his own glory ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 14:16\index{44 Acts:ch.  14, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} but such as has joined with it a most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and powerful bounding\index{Providence:governing all ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 76:10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  76, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 19:28\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  19, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} and otherwise ordering and\index{Providence:ordering:all things for his glory and believers' good ``f10!} governing of them, in a manifold dispensation\index{Providence:God's dispensation ``f10!}, to His own holy\index{God's attributes:holy:ends ``f10!} ends;\footnote{\ Genesis 50:20\index{01 Genesis:ch.  50, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 10:6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} yet so, as the sinfulness thereof proceeded only\index{Sin:proceeds only from man, not God ``f10!} from the creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, and not from God, who, being most holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most ``f10!} and righteous, neither\index{God's attributes:righteousness ``f10!} is, nor can be, the author or approver\index{Sin:God not author or approver of ``f10!} of sin.\footnote{\ James 1:13-14, 17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  13-14, 17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:16\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 50:21\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
5.5\ \ The most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!}, righteous, and gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} God does oftentimes leave for a season His\index{Temptation:left by God for a season ``f10!} own children to manifold temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, and the corruption of the\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:flesh ``f10!}ir\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:hearts ``f10!} own hearts\index{Heart:corrupt ``f10!}, to chastise\index{Believers:chastened by God ``f10!} them for their former sins, or to discover\index{Temptation:exposes (discovers) corruption ``f10!} unto them the hidden strength of\index{Sin:original:hidden strength of corruption ``f10!} corruption, and\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:hidden ``f10!} deceitfulness\index{Deceitfulness:of heart ``f10!} of their hearts, that\index{Heart:deceitful ``f10!} they may be humbled\index{Humility:before God ``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 32:25-26, 31\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  32, v.  25-26, 31, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 24:1\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  24, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and, to raise them to a more close and constant dependence\index{Temptation:increase dependence on God ``f10!} for their support upon Himself, and to make them more watchful against\index{Temptation:watchfulness required to avoid ``f10!} all future occasions of sin, and for sundry other just and holy\index{God's attributes:holy:nature ``f10!} ends.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 12:7-9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 73 throughout, Psalm 77:1-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  77, v.   1-12, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 14:66 to the end, with John 21:15-17\index{43 John:ch.  21, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
5.6\ \ As for those wicked\index{blindness, spiritual ``f10!} and ungodly\index{Unbelievers:ungodly ``f10!} men whom God, as a righteous Judge, for\index{God's attributes:judge ``f10!} former sins, does blind and harden\index{Heart:hardened ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 1:24, 26, 28\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  24, 26, 28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:29\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} and exposes\index{Punishment:exposure to consequences of sin ``f10!} them to such objects as their corruption makes\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:lustful ``f10!} occasions of sin;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 2:30\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   2, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 8:12-13\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   8, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} and, withal, gives them over to their own lusts\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!}, the temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of the world, and the power of Satan\index{Satan:power of ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Psalm 81:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:10\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby it comes to pass that they harden themselves, even under those means which God uses for the softening\index{Providence:hardens some, softens others ``f10!} of others.\footnote{\ Exodus 7:3\index{02 Exodus:ch.   7, v.   3, pg. ``f30!} with Exodus 8:15, 32\index{02 Exodus:ch.   8, v.  15, 32, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 2:15-16\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 8:14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:7-8\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 6:9-10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!} with Acts 28:26-27\index{44 Acts:ch.  28, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
5.7\ \ As the providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} of God does in general reach to all creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, so after a most special manner, it takes care of His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, and disposes\index{Providence:God disposes all for good of his Church ``f10!} all things to the good thereof.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 9:8-9\index{30 Amos:ch.   9, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 43:3-5, 14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  43, v.   3-5, 14, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 6 -- Of the Fall of Man, of Sin, and of the Punishment thereof} \index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!}6.1\ \ Our first parents\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!}, being seduced\index{Temptation:Satan's seduction of our first parents ``f10!} by the subtilty\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} and temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of Satan, sinned, in eating the forbidden\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} fruit.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:13\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 11:3\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} This their sin God was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}, according to His wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy counsel, to\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} permit\index{Sin:God purposes and permits for his own glory ``f10!}, having purposed to order it to His own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 11:32\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
6.2\ \ By this sin they fell\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} from their original righteousness and\index{Mankind:created:original righteousness ``f10!} communion, with\index{Communion:with God ``f10!} God,\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} and so became dead\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!} in sin,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and wholly defiled in all\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:defiled in all parts and faculties ``f10!} the parts and faculties of soul\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:faculties of the soul ``f10!} and body.\footnote{\ Titus 1:15\index{56 Titus:ch.   1, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 17:9\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10-19, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
6.3\ \ They being the root\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} of all mankind, the\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} of this sin was imputed,\index{Imputation:of Adam's sin ``f10!}\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!} and Genesis 2:16-17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!} and Acts 17:26\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  26, pg. ``f30!} with Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}, 15-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 15-19, pg. ``f30!} and 1 Corinthians 15:21-22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}, 49\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  21-22, 49, pg. ``f30!}.} and the same death\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!} in sin and corrupted\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:conveyed from Adam ``f10!} nature conveyed, to all their posterity descending from them by ordinary\index{Sin:original:by ordinary generation ``f10!} generation.\footnote{\ Psalm 51:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 5:3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   5, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 14:4\index{18 Job:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Job 15:14\index{18 Job:ch.  15, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
6.4\ \ From this original corruption, whereby\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} we are utterly indisposed\index{Sin:original:utterly indisposed ``f10!}, disabled\index{Sin:original:utterly unable and unwilling to do will of God ``f10!}, and made opposite to all good,\footnote{\ Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:21\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and wholly inclined\index{Sin:original:inclined to do evil ``f10!} to all evil,\footnote{\ Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 8:21\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} do proceed all\index{Sin:original:proceeds all transgressions ``f10!} actual transgressions\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}.\footnote{\ James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
6.5\ \ This corruption\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} of nature, during this life, does remain in those that are regenerated\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John 1:8, 10\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 17-18, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  14, 17-18, 23, pg. ``f30!}; James 3:2\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 20:9\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  20, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} and although it be, through Christ, pardoned and\index{Regeneration:pardoned of sin ``f10!} mortified\index{Sin:mortified ``f10!}, yet both itself and all the motions thereof are truly\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} and properly sin.\footnote{\ Romans 7:5, 7-8, 25\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   5, 7-8, 25, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
6.6\ \ Every sin, both original and actual, being a transgression of\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} the righteous law\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} of God, and contrary thereunto,\footnote{\ 1 John 3:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} does, in its own nature, bring guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} upon the sinner;\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, 19, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby he is bound over to the wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and curse of the\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!} law,\footnote{\ Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and so made subject to death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 6:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} with all miseries\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!} spiritual,\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} temporal,\index{Judgement:temporal ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Lamentations 3:39\index{25 Lamentations:ch.   3, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} and eternal.\footnote{\ Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 1:9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 7 -- Of God's Covenant with Man} \index{Covenant:of God with man ``f10!}7.1\ \ The distance\index{Mankind:great distance between him and God ``f10!} between God and the creature\index{creatures ``f10!} is so great, that although reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!} creatures do owe obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} unto Him as their Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things ``f10!}, yet they could never have any fruition of Him as their blessedness and\index{Believers:blessed in/by God ``f10!} reward\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!}, but by some voluntary condescension\index{God's attributes:condescension, voluntary ``f10!} on God's part, which He has been pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to express by way of covenant\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 40:13-17\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  40, v.  13-17, pg. ``f30!}; Job 9:32-33\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.  32-33, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 2:25\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 113:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 113, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 100:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 35:7-8\index{18 Job:ch.  35, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
 7.2\ \ The first covenant made\index{Covenant:first:made with man ``f10!} with man was a covenant of works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} wherein life was promised to\index{Covenant:first:promised life ``f10!} Adam, and in him to\index{Adam:covenant made with him ``f10!} his posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12-20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} upon condition\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!} of perfect and personal obedience\index{Covenant:works:perfect obedience required ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
7.3\ \ Man by his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} having made himself incapable\index{Covenant:works:Adam:incapable of life after his sin ``f10!} of life by that covenant, the\index{Covenant:first:broken ``f10!} Lord was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to make a second\index{Covenant:second ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:15\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 42:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} commonly called the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}; wherein He freely\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!} offers unto sinners life and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} by Jesus Christ, requiring\index{Salvation:faith alone required ``f10!} of them faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} in Him, that they may be saved,\footnote{\ Mark 16:15\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:6, 9\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   6, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:11\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and promising to\index{Holy Spirit:promising to believers ``f10!} give unto all those that are ordained unto\index{Predestination:unto life ``f10!} life His Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, to make them willing and able to\index{Conversion:renewal of the will ``f10!} believe.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:44\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}{}-45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44-45, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
7.4\ \ This covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} is frequently set forth in Scripture by the name of a Testament\index{Covenant:testament ``f10!}, in reference to the death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} of Jesus Christ the Testator\index{Covenant:grace:Jesus testator ``f10!}, and to the everlasting inheritance\index{Believers:inheritance:everlasting ``f10!}, with all things belonging to it, therein bequeathed.\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
7.5\ \ This covenant was\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!} differently administered in the time of the law, and in the time of the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}:\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6-9, pg. ``f30!}.} under the law, it was administered by promises\index{Covenant:promises ``f10!}, prophecies\index{Covenant:prophecies ``f10!}, sacrifices\index{Ceremonial law:sacrifices ``f10!}, circumcision\index{circumcision ``f10!}, the paschal\index{paschal lamb ``f10!} lamb\index{lamb, paschal ``f10!}, and other types\index{types, OT ``f10!} and ordinances delivered\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:signified Christ ``f10!} to the people of the Jews, all\index{Jews:OT ordinances ``f10!} fore-signifying\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} Christ to come:\footnote{\ Hebrews 8-10\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 8-10, pg. ``f30!} chapters, Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:11-12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} which were, for that time, sufficient and\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:sufficient for that time ``f10!} efficacious\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:efficacious ``f10!}, through the operation\index{Holy Spirit:operations:saving ``f10!} of the Spirit, to\index{Holy Spirit:instructs the elect ``f10!} instruct and build up the\index{Holy Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} in faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ, as Messiah ``f10!} in the promised\index{Jesus:Messiah promised ``f10!} Messiah,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:1-4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 11:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:56\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  56, pg. ``f30!}.} by whom they had full remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins ``f10!} of sins, and eternal salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}; and is called, the Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:7-9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   7-9, 14, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
7.6\ \ Under the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, when Christ, the substance,\footnote{\ Colossians 2:17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} was exhibited, the\index{Covenant:grace:exhibited ``f10!} ordinances in\index{Church:furnished with:ordinances of God ``f10!} which this covenant is dispensed are\index{Covenant:new:ways dispensed ``f10!} the preaching of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}, and the administration\index{Church:true:sacraments administered ``f10!} of the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of Baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-25, pg. ``f30!}.} which, though fewer in number, and administered with\index{Sacraments:to be:administered with simplicity ``f10!} more simplicity, and less outward\index{Sacraments:NT less outward glory than OT ``f10!} glory; yet, in them, it is held forth in more fulness\index{Covenant:new:more fulness ``f10!}, evidence, and spiritual efficacy,\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  22, pg. ``f30!} to 28; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}.} to all nations\index{Gospel:to all nations ``f10!}, both Jews and\index{Jews:called ``f10!} Gentiles\index{Gentiles:called ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  15-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and is called the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 22:20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} There are not therefore two covenants of\index{Covenant:grace:one only ``f10!} grace, differing in substance\index{Covenant:grace:one, but differ in substance ``f10!}, but one and the same, under various dispensations\index{Covenant:dispensations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:14, 16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  14, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1-23, 30\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  21-23, 30, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 32:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   1, pg. ``f30!} with Romans 4:3, 6, 16-17, 23-24\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   3, 6, 16-17, 23-24, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 8 -- Of Christ the Mediator} \index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}8.1\ \ It pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} God, in His eternal purpose\index{Predestination:eternal purpose ``f10!}, to choose and ordain the\index{Predestination:Jesus as mediator ``f10!} Lord Jesus, His only begotten\index{Jesus:begotten by the Father ``f10!} Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, to be the Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} between God and man;\footnote{\ Isaiah 42:1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:19-20\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} the Prophet\index{Jesus:prophet:office ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 3:22\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} Priest\index{Jesus:priest ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:5-6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} and King\index{Jesus:King ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 2:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:33\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} the Head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} and Saviour\index{Jesus:saviour of the Church ``f10!} of His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} the Heir\index{Jesus:heir of all things ``f10!} of all things,\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and Judge of\index{Jesus:judge:of world ``f10!} the world:\footnote{\ Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} unto whom He did from all eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!} give a people, to be His seed\index{Election:God's seed ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 17:6\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 22:30\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 53:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and to be by Him in time redeemed\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!}, called, justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!}, sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, and glorified\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:glorification ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 55:4-5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 1:30\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
8.2\ \ The Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God, the second person in\index{Jesus:second person in Trinity ``f10!} the Trinity\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!}, being very and eternal God\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}, of one substance and equal with the\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!} Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, did, when the fulness of time\index{Jesus:incarnation:in fulness of time ``f10!} was come, take upon Him man's nature,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:20\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} with all the essential properties and\index{Jesus:human nature:essential properties ``f10!} common infirmities thereof\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:infirmities ``f10!}, yet without sin:\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 16-17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, 16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} being conceived by\index{Jesus:conceived:by the power of the Holy Spirit ``f10!} the power of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, in the womb\index{Jesus:conceived:in womb of virgin Mary ``f10!} of the virgin\index{Jesus:born of virgin Mary ``f10!} Mary\index{Mary, mother of Jesus ``f10!}, of her substance\index{Jesus:conceived:of Mary's substance ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 1:27, 31, 35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  27, 31, 35, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} So that two whole, perfect, and distinct natures\index{Jesus:two distinct natures ``f10!}, the Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!} and the manhood\index{Jesus:human nature:manhood ``f10!}, were inseparably\index{Jesus:human nature:inseparable from divine, one person ``f10!} joined together in one person, without conversion, composition\index{God's attributes:being:no composition ``f10!}, or confusion\index{God's attributes:being:no confusion ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 1:35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:9\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 3:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} Which person is very God, and very man, yet one Christ, the only Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} between God and man.\footnote{\ Romans 1:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
8.3\ \ The Lord Jesus, in His human nature thus\index{Jesus:human nature:united with divine ``f10!} united to the divine, was sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} and anointed\index{Jesus:anointed with Holy Spirit ``f10!} with the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, above measure,\footnote{\ Psalm 45:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:3\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}.} having in Him all the treasures of wisdom and\index{Jesus:wisdom, treasures of ``f10!} knowledge;\index{Jesus:human nature:all knowledge ``f10!}\footnote{\ Colossians 2:3\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} in whom it pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!} that all fulness should\index{Jesus:fulness of Godhead dwells ``f10!} dwell;\footnote{\ Colossians 1:19\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} to the end that, being holy\index{Jesus:holy ``f10!}, harmless\index{Jesus:harmless ``f10!}, undefiled\index{Jesus:undefiled ``f10!}, and full of grace\index{Jesus:full of grace ``f10!} and truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 7:26\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} He might be thoroughly furnished\index{Jesus:mediator:fully furnished to execute office ``f10!} to execute the office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} of a mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} and surety\index{Jesus:surety for the elect ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 10:38\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} Which office He took not unto Himself, but was thereunto called by His Father,\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} who put all power\index{Jesus:almighty power ``f10!} and judgment into\index{Jesus:judge:assigned by Father ``f10!} His hand, and gave Him commandment\index{Jesus:commanded by the Father ``f10!} to execute the same\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 5:22, 27\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  22, 27, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:36\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
8.4\ \ This office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} the Lord Jesus did most willingly\index{Jesus:humiliation:willingly undertaken ``f10!} undertake;\footnote{\ Psalm 40:7-8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  40, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews 10:5-10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   5-10, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:18\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} which that He might discharge, He\index{Jesus:discharged:his duties ``f10!} was made under the law,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and did perfectly fulfil\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!} it,\footnote{\ Matthew 3:15\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip
