\section{Chapter 9 -- Of Free Will} \index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!}9.1\ \ God has endued the\index{Causation:will of creatures:natural liberty ``f10!} will of man with that natural liberty, that\index{Liberty:natural ``f10!} is neither forced, nor by any absolute\index{Mankind:human will, natural liberty ``f10!} necessity of\index{Liberty:not absolute necessity to good or evil ``f10!} nature determined to good or evil.\footnote{\ Matthew 17:12\index{40 Matthew:ch.  17, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 30:19\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  30, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
9.2\ \ Man, in his state of innocency, had\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence ``f10!} freedom and\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!} power to will and to do that which was good, and well pleasing\index{Mankind:created:initially able to please God ``f10!} to God;\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} but yet, mutably\index{Mankind:created:mutable ``f10!}, so that he might fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} from it.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:16-17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
9.3\ \ Man, by his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} into a state of sin, has wholly lost all ability of\index{Sin:original:inability to:do anything good ``f10!} will to any spiritual good\index{Sin:original:lost all spiritual good ``f10!} accompanying salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; John 15:5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} so as, a natural man, being altogether averse from that good,\footnote{\ Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} and dead in sin\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, 5, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} is not able, by his own strength, to\index{Conversion:not by own strength ``f10!} convert himself\index{Conversion:not of self ``f10!}, or to prepare himself thereunto.\footnote{\ John 6:44\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}, 65\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, 65, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2-5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:3-5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.}    
\bigskip
9.4\ \ When God converts\index{Conversion:conversion ``f10!} a sinner, and translates\index{Conversion:translated into state of grace ``f10!} him into the state of grace\index{Grace:state:translation into at conversion ``f10!}, He frees\index{Believers:freed from:guilt of sin ``f10!} him from his natural bondage under\index{Sin:bondage to ``f10!} sin;\footnote{\ Colossians 1:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:34\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}, 36\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  34, 36, pg. ``f30!}.} and, by His grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} alone, enables\index{Sanctification:enabled by:grace ``f10!} him freely\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!} to will and to do that which is spiritually good;\index{Good works:spiritual services ``f10!}\footnote{\ Philippians 2:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:18, 22\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  18, 22, pg. ``f30!}.} yet so, as that by reason of his remaining corruption, he\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} does not perfectly, nor only, will that which is good, but does also will that which is evil.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  15, 18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19, 21, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  15, 18-19, 21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.}    
\bigskip
9.5\ \ The will of man is made perfectly and immutably\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} free to do good alone, in the state of glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:light ``f10!} only.\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:13\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 24\index{65 Jude:v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 10 -- Of Effectual Calling} \index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}10.1\ \ All those whom God has predestinated\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!} unto life, and those only, He is pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} in His appointed and accepted time\index{Salvation:at appointed time ``f10!} effectually to\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} call,\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip
10.2\ \ This effectual call\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} is of God's free and special grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} alone, not from anything at all foreseen\index{Predestination:not based on God's foresight:of anything in man ``f10!} in man,\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 1:9\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:4-5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:4-5, 8-9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   4-5, 8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} who is altogether passive\index{Effectual call:mankind passive ``f10!} therein, until being quickened\index{Conversion:quickened to new life ``f10!} and renewed by\index{Conversion:renewed by Holy Spirit ``f10!} the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 2:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} he is thereby enabled to answer\index{Effectual call:enables person to:freely answer call ``f10!} this call, and to embrace the grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} offered and\index{Effectual call:enables person to:embrace grace ``f10!} conveyed in it.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:25\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:37\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
10.3\ \ Elect\index{Infants:elect, dying in infancy ``f10!} infants, dying in infancy, are regenerated\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}, and saved by Christ\index{Salvation:by Christ ``f10!} through the Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:applies:regeneration ``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke 18:1\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!} and Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}{}-39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:3\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:12\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; and Romans 8:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   9, pg. ``f30!} compared.} who works\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!} when, and where, and how He pleases\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}:\footnote{\ John 3:8\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} so also, are all other elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} persons who are uncapable\index{Infants:incapable of being outwardly called ``f10!} of being outwardly called\index{Preaching:outward call ``f10!} by the ministry of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 5:12\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
10.4\ \ Others, not elected\index{Election:some not chosen ``f10!}, although they may be called by the ministry of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 22:14\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and may have some common operations\index{Holy Spirit:operations:common ``f10!} of the Spirit,\footnote{\ Matthew 7:22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 13:20-21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:4-5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} yet they never truly\index{Unbelievers:non-elect never truly come to Jesus ``f10!} come unto Christ, and therefore cannot be saved:\index{Salvation:not in other religions ``f10!}\footnote{\ John 6:64-66\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  64-66, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:24\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} much less can men, not professing the\index{Profession:absent ``f10!} Christian religion\index{Profession:of false religion ``f10!}, be saved in any other way whatsoever, be they never so diligent to\index{God's law:diligence in application ``f10!} frame their\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!} lives according to the light of nature, and the law of that religion they do profess.\footnote{\ Acts 4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:22\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:3\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} And to assert and maintain that they may, is very pernicious\index{Salvation:outside of Christ, pernicious and detestable claim ``f10!}, and to be detested.\footnote{\ 2 John 9-11\index{63 2 John:v. 9-11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 16:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 1:6-8\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 11 -- Of Justification} \index{Justification:justification ``f10!}11.1\ \ Those whom God effectually calls\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}, He also freely justifies\index{Justification:freely by God ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; \section{Chapter 13 -- Of Sanctification} \index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}13.1\ \ They who are once effectually called\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} and regenerated\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}, having a new heart\index{Heart:new:regenerate ``f10!} and a new spirit created in them\index{Conversion:created in Christ ``f10!}, are further sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, really and personally\index{Sanctification:personal ``f10!}, through the virtue\index{Jesus:vicarious atonement ``f10!} of Christ's death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} and resurrection,\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 6:11\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip
13.2\ \ This sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} is throughout, in the whole man;\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 5:23\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet imperfect in\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!} this life, there abiding still\index{Sin:remnants in believers ``f10!} some remnants\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} of corruption in every part:\footnote{\ 1 John 1:10\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:12\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} whence arises a continual and irreconcilable war; the flesh lusting\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!} against the Spirit, and the Spirit against\index{Holy Spirit:at war with believers' lusts and flesh ``f10!} the flesh.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:11\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
13.3\ \ In which war, although the remaining corruption, for\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} a time, may much prevail\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 7:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet through the continual supply\index{Sanctification:supply of strength from Holy Spirit ``f10!} of strength from the sanctifying\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!}, the regenerate\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!} part does overcome\index{Sin:overcoming ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:15-16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} and so, the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} grow in\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in grace ``f10!} grace,\footnote{\ 2 Peter 3:18\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} perfecting holiness\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} in the fear of\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!} God.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 14 -- Of Saving Faith} \index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\index{Faith:saving ``f10!}14.1\ \ The grace of faith\index{Faith:given by grace ``f10!}, whereby the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} are enabled to believe\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:enables belief ``f10!} to the saving of\index{Salvation:by working of Holy Spirit ``f10!} their souls,\index{Holy Spirit:applies:faith ``f10!}\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:39\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} is the work of the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!} in their hearts;\index{Heart:new:enlightened ``f10!}\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 4:13\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} and is ordinarily wrought by the\index{Preaching:convincing and converting sinners ``f10!} ministry of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 17\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, 17, pg. ``f30!}.} by which also, and by the administration\index{Sacraments:grace:administered ``f10!} of the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, and prayer, it\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!} is increased and strengthened\index{Sacraments:strengthening ordinances ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:5\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:16\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
14.2\ \ By this faith\index{Faith:believes Scripture to be word of God ``f10!}, a Christian believes to\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} be true whatsoever is revealed in the Word, for\index{Scripture:word of God:standard for:life ``f10!} the authority of God Himself speaking therein;\footnote{\ John 4:42\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:10\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 24:14\index{44 Acts:ch.  24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and acts differently upon that which each particular passage thereof contains; yielding\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} obedience to the commands\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 16:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} trembling at the threatenings\index{God's law:threatenings for disobedience ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah 66:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  66, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and embracing the promises\index{Salvation:promises made ``f10!} of God for this life, and that which is to come.\footnote{\ Hebrews 11:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 4:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} But the principal\index{Faith:principal acts of ``f10!} acts of saving faith\index{Faith:saving ``f10!} are accepting\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, receiving, and\index{Faith:instrument:for receiving Christ ``f10!} resting upon\index{Faith:resting on Christ ``f10!} Christ alone for justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!}, sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, and eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!}, by virtue of the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:20\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
14.3\ \ This faith is different in degrees\index{Faith:degrees of ``f10!}, weak or strong;\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:13-14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:19-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 6:30\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 8:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   8, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} may be often and many ways assailed\index{Faith:assailed ``f10!}, and weakened\index{Faith:weak ``f10!}, but gets the victory\index{Faith:victorious ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 22:31-32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  31-32, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} growing up in\index{Assurance:growing ``f10!} many to the attainment of a full assurance through\index{Assurance:of faith ``f10!} Christ,\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} who is both the author\index{Jesus:author of a believer's faith ``f10!} and finisher\index{Jesus:finisher of a believer's faith ``f10!} of our faith.\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 15 -- Of Repentance unto Life} \index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!}15.1\ \ Repentance\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!} unto life is an evangelical grace\index{Grace:evangelical ``f10!},\footnote{\ Zechariah 12:10\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 11:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} the doctrine whereof\index{Doctrine:Gospel ``f10!} is to be preached by every\index{Preaching:call to repentance ``f10!} minister\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, as well as that of faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} in Christ.\footnote{\ Luke 24:47\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  47, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 1:15\index{41 Mark:ch.   1, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:21\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
15.2\ \ By it, a sinner, out of the sight and sense not only of the danger\index{Repentance:apprehension of danger of sin ``f10!}, but also of the filthiness\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} and odiousness\index{Sin:odious before God ``f10!} of his sins, as contrary to the holy\index{God's law:holy ``f10!} nature and righteous law\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} of God; and upon the apprehension\index{Repentance:apprehension of God's mercy ``f10!} of his mercy in\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} Christ to such as are penitent\index{Repentance:penitence ``f10!}, so grieves for\index{Sin:grief and hatred of ``f10!}, and hates\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} his sins, as to turn from them all unto God,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 18:30-31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  18, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 36:31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 30:22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  30, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:18\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Joel 2:12\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 5:15\index{30 Amos:ch.   5, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:128\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 128, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} purposing\index{Repentance:purposing to walk with God ``f10!} and endeavouring to walk with\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:endeavoring ``f10!} Him in all the ways of His commandments\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 119:6, 59, 106\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   6, 59, 106, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:6\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 23:25\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  23, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
15.3\ \ Although repentance be\index{Repentance:required for pardon ``f10!} not to be rested in, as any satisfaction for sin\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!}, or any cause of the pardon the\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons ``f10!}reof,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}{}-32\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31-32, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 16:61-63\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  16, v.  61-63, pg. ``f30!}.} which is the act of God's free grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} in Christ;\footnote{\ Hosea 14:2\index{28 Hosea:ch.  14, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 4\index{28 Hosea:ch.  14, v.   2, 4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} yet is it of such necessity to\index{Repentance:necessity ``f10!} all sinners, that none may expect pardon without it.\footnote{\ Luke 13:3, 5\index{42 Luke:ch.  13, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:30-31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
15.4\ \ As there is no sin so small, but it deserves\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!} damnation\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 6:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:36\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} so there is no sin so great, that it can bring damnation upon those who truly\index{Repentance:for all sins ``f10!} repent.\footnote{\ Isaiah 55:7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 1:16, 18\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  16, 18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
15.5\ \ Men ought not to content themselves with a general repentance, but\index{Repentance:for all sins ``f10!} it is every man's duty to endeavour\index{Repentance:duty to endeavour ``f10!} to repent of his particular sins, particularly.\footnote{\ Psalm 19:13\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 19:8\index{42 Luke:ch.  19, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:13, 15\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  13, 15, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
15.6\ \ As every man is bound to make private confession\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} of his sins to God, praying for\index{Prayer:for pardon of sin ``f10!} the pardon the\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons ``f10!}reof;\index{Forgiveness:beg pardon for ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 51:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5, 7, 9, 14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4-5, 7, 9, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 32:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} upon which, and the forsaking\index{Repentance:forsaking sin ``f10!} of them, he shall find mercy:\index{Mercy:on confession ``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs 28:13\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  28, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} so, he that scandalizes\index{Scandalous behaviour:to be confessed ``f10!} his brother, or the Church of Christ\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, ought to be willing, by a private or public confession, and sorrow\index{Confession:sorrow for sin ``f10!} for his sin, to declare his\index{Repentance:public declaration ``f10!} repentance to\index{Repentance:to those offended ``f10!} those that are offended,\index{Confession:to those offended ``f10!}\footnote{\ James 5:16\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:3-4\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 7:19\index{06 Joshua:ch.   7, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51.} who are thereupon to be reconciled\index{Confession:to be reconciled to God ``f10!} to him, and in love to\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!} receive him.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 2:8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 16 -- Of Good Works} \index{Good works:definition ``f10!}16.1\ \ Good works\index{Good works:definition ``f10!} are only such as God has commanded in His\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} holy Word\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!},\footnote{\ Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 12:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:21\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and not such as, without the warrant\index{Good works:not devised by men without warrant ``f10!} thereof, are devised\index{Good works:not devised by men ``f10!} by men, out of blind zeal, or\index{Good works:not out of blind zeal ``f10!} upon any pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of good intention\index{Good works:not by good intentions ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 29:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  29, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; John 16:2\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 15:21\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}{}-23\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}.}    
\bigskip
16.2\ \ These good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!}, done in obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} to God's commandments\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}, are the fruits\index{Good works:fruit of salvation ``f10!} and evidences of a true and lively\index{Faith:lively ``f10!} faith:\footnote{\ James 2:18, 22\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  18, 22, pg. ``f30!}.} and by them believers manifest\index{Good works:believers manifest thankfulness ``f10!} their thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 116:12-13\index{19 Psalms:ch. 116, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:9\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} strengthen their assurance\index{Assurance:strengthened ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:5-10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5-10, pg. ``f30!}.} edify\index{Good works:edify other Christians ``f10!} their brethren\index{Believers:to build up fellow believers ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 9:2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   9, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:16\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} adorn the profession\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!},\footnote{\ Titus 2:5, 9-12\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.   5, 9-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} stop the mouths\index{Good works:stop mouths of adversaries ``f10!} of the adversaries,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:15\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} God,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:12\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 1:1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; John 15:8\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} whose workmanship\index{Believers:God's workmanship ``f10!} they are, created in Christ\index{Conversion:created in Christ ``f10!} Jesus thereunto;\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} that, having their fruit unto holiness\index{Believers:holy:made perfect at death ``f10!}, they may have the end, eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 6:22\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
16.3\ \ Their ability to do\index{Good works:only in Holy Spirit ``f10!} good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!} is not at all of themselves, but wholly from the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 15:4-5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} And that they may be enabled thereunto\index{Good works:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!}, besides the graces\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} they have already received, there is required an actual influence of the same Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, to work in them to will and to do of His good pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Philippians 2:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:5\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} yet are they not hereupon to grow negligent, as\index{Good works:not be negligent ``f10!} if they were not bound to perform any duty, unless\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} upon a special motion of the Spirit; but\index{Holy Spirit:helps believers do good works ``f10!} they ought to be diligent in\index{Grace:diligent use of means ``f10!} stirring up the grace of\index{Grace:in believers:to be stirred up ``f10!} God that is in them.\footnote{\ Philippians 2:12\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:3, 5, 10-11\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   3, 5, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 64:7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 1:6\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:6-7\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 20-21\index{65 Jude:v. 20-21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
16.4\ \ They, who in their obedience\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!} attain to the greatest height which is possible in this life, are so far from being able to supererogate\index{Good works:believers cannot supererogate (do more than required) ``f10!}, and to do more than God requires, as\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} that they fall short\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!} of much which in duty they are bound to do.\footnote{\ Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Job 9:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
16.5\ \ We cannot, by our best works, merit\index{Salvation:not by:works ``f10!} pardon of sin, or\index{Good works:not merit pardon of sin ``f10!} eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!} at the hand of God, by reason of the great disproportion\index{Good works:great disproportion compared with glory ``f10!} that is between them and the glory to\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:state of ``f10!} come; and the infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:separation from creatures ``f10!} distance\index{Mankind:great distance between him and God ``f10!} that is between us and God, whom, by them, we can neither profit, nor satisfy for\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!} the debt\index{Forgiveness:of debtors ``f10!} of our former sins,\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:2, 4, 6\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   2, 4, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5-7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 16:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Job 22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 35:7-8\index{18 Job:ch.  35, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} but when we have done all we can, we have done but our duty, and are\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} unprofitable servants\index{Good works:duty of unprofitable servants ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and because, as they are good, they proceed from His\index{Good works:only in Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit;\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2-23\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} and as they are wrought by us, they are defiled, and\index{Good works:defiled ``f10!} mixed\index{Good works:mixed with weakness and imperfection ``f10!} with so much weakness and\index{Sanctification:weaknesses and imperfections remain ``f10!} imperfection, that they cannot endure the severity\index{Good works:cannot endure severity of God's judgement ``f10!} of God's judgment\index{Judgement:severe ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 130:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.}    
\bigskip
16.6\ \ Yet notwithstanding, the persons of believers being accepted through\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!} Christ, their good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!} also are accepted in Him\index{Good works:accepted in Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 28:38\index{02 Exodus:ch.  28, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 4:4\index{01 Genesis:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews 11:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} not as though they were in this life wholly unblameable and unreproveable\index{Good works:not unreproveable ``f10!} in God's sight;\footnote{\ Job 9:20\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 143:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 143, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} but that He, looking upon them in His Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, is pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to accept and reward\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!} that which is sincere\index{Good works:sincere accepted by God ``f10!}, although accompanied with many weaknesses\index{Sanctification:weaknesses and imperfections remain ``f10!} and imperfections\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 8:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
16.7\ \ Works done\index{Good works:not merit pardon of sin ``f10!} by unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate ``f10!} men, although, for the matter of them, they may be things which God commands, and of\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:not salvific ``f10!} good use both to themselves and others:\footnote{\ 2 Kings 10:30-31\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  10, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} And yet, their neglect of them\index{Good works:not be negligent ``f10!} is more sinful, and displeasing unto God.\footnote{\ Psalm 14:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; \section{Chapter 17 -- Of the Perseverance of the Saints} \index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!}\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}17.1\ \ They, whom God has accepted in His\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!} Beloved\index{Jesus:beloved of the Father ``f10!}, effectually called\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}, and sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} by His Spirit, can\index{Holy Spirit:applies:sanctification ``f10!} neither totally\index{Assurance:never fall from being saved ``f10!}, nor finally, fall away from the state of grace\index{Grace:state:fall from ``f10!}: but shall certainly persevere\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!} therein to the end, and be eternally\index{Salvation:eternal for those effectually called ``f10!} saved.\footnote{\ Philippians 1:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, 9, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
17.2\ \ This perseverance\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!} of the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} depends not upon their\index{Perseverance:depends not on person's will ``f10!} own free will, but upon the immutability\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} of the decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of election\index{Election:decree of ``f10!}, flowing from the free and unchangeable\index{God's attributes:unchangeable ``f10!} love of God\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!} the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 2:18-19\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} upon the efficacy\index{Perseverance:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} of the merit and\index{Jesus:obedience:merit of ``f10!} intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!} of Jesus Christ;\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  10, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  12-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33, pg. ``f30!} to the end, John 17:11, 24\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  11, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} the abiding of\index{Holy Spirit:abiding in believers ``f10!} the Spirit, and of the seed of God\index{Believers:seed of God planted within ``f10!} within them;\footnote{\ John 14:16-17\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} and the nature of the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Jeremiah 32:40\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  32, v.  40, pg. ``f30!}.} from all which arises also the certainty and infallibility\index{Covenant:grace:infallible ``f10!} thereof.\footnote{\ John 10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:3\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:19\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
17.3\ \ Nevertheless, they may, through the temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of Satan and of\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} the world, the prevalence of corruption remaining\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} in them, and the neglect of the means\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!} of their preservation\index{Perseverance:means neglected ``f10!}, fall into grievous sins\index{Temptation:fall into grievous sins ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 26:70, 72, 74\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  70, 72, 74, pg. ``f30!}.} and, for a time, continue therein:\footnote{\ Psalm 51 title and 14.} whereby they incur\index{Believers:may experience God's displeasure for sin ``f10!} God's displeasure,\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:5, 7, 9\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   5, 7, 9, pg. ``f30!}; \section{Chapter 18 -- Of the Assurance of Grace and Salvation} \index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!}\index{Salvation:assurance of ``f10!}18.1\ \ Although hypocrites\index{hypocrisy ``f10!} and other unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate ``f10!} men may vainly deceive\index{Deceitfulness:of self ``f10!} themselves with false hopes\index{Hope:false ``f10!}, and carnal presumptions\index{presumption ``f10!} of being in the favour\index{Unbelievers:presumptuous about favour with God ``f10!} of God, and estate of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!};\footnote{\ Job 8:13-14\index{18 Job:ch.   8, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18-19, 21, 24\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, 18-19, 21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:13\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and may rejoice in the hope of\index{Hope:of glory of God, rejoice in ``f10!} the glory of God, which\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:everlasting ``f10!} hope shall\index{Hope:certain ``f10!} never make them ashamed\index{Believers:never made ashamed by God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 5:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   2, 5, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
18.2\ \ This certainty is not a bare conjectural\index{Assurance:not bare conjecture ``f10!} and probable persuasion\index{Assurance:not probable persuasion ``f10!}, grounded upon a fallible hope;\index{Hope:fallible ``f10!}\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:11, 19\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11, 19, pg. ``f30!}.} but an infallible\index{Assurance:infallible ``f10!} assurance of faith\index{Assurance:of faith ``f10!}, founded\index{Assurance:founded on God's promises ``f10!} upon the divine\index{Salvation:founded on divine truth ``f10!} truth of the promises\index{Salvation:promises made ``f10!} of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} the inward evidence\index{Assurance:inward evidence ``f10!} of those graces\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} unto which these promises\index{Assurance:promises of God ``f10!} are made,\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:4-5, 10-11\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   4-5, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} the testimony of the Spirit\index{Assurance:Holy Spirit witnesses with our spirits ``f10!} of adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!} witnessing with our spirits\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:bears witness to our spirits ``f10!} that we are the children of God:\footnote{\ Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} which Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:earnest of believers' inheritance ``f10!} is the earnest of\index{Believers:inheritance:earnest of ``f10!} our inheritance\index{Believers:inheritance:everlasting ``f10!}, whereby we are sealed to the\index{Salvation:sealed to the day of redemption ``f10!} day of redemption\index{Redemption:day of ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip
18.3\ \ This infallible\index{Assurance:infallible ``f10!} assurance does\index{Assurance:believer may await ``f10!} not so belong to the essence of faith\index{Faith:essence of ``f10!}, but that a true believer may wait long, and conflict with many difficulties\index{Assurance:believer may experience difficulties ``f10!} before he be partaker of it:\footnote{\ 1 John 5:13\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 14:17\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 15:13\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:3-4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 4:6-7\index{19 Psalms:ch.   4, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:32\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.} so far is it from inclining men to looseness.\footnote{\ 1 John 2:1-2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:1-2\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 2:11-12, 14\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.  11-12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, 12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 130:4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:6-7\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
18.4\ \ True believers may\index{Assurance:believer may not have at all times ``f10!} have the assurance of their salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} divers ways shaken\index{Assurance:shaken at times ``f10!}, diminished, and intermitted; as, by negligence\index{Assurance:negligence in preserving ``f10!} in preserving\index{Perseverance:means neglected ``f10!} of it, by falling\index{God's law:broken daily by believers ``f10!} into some special sin, which wounds the conscience\index{Conscience:wounded ``f10!} and grieves the\index{Sin:grieves the Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit; by some sudden\index{Temptation:sudden ``f10!} or vehement\index{Temptation:vehement ``f10!} temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, by God's withdrawing the light of His countenance\index{Believers:chastened by God ``f10!}, and suffering even such as fear Him\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!} to walk in darkness\index{darkness, spiritual ``f10!} and to have no light:\footnote{\ Song of Solomon 5:2-3, 6\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch.   5, v.   2-3, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}{}-31\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 50:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  50, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} yet are they never so utterly destitute\index{Assurance:never destitute ``f10!} of that seed of God\index{Believers:seed of God planted within ``f10!}, and life of faith\index{Faith:living by ``f10!}, that love of Christ\index{Love:of Christ ``f10!} and the brethren\index{Believers:to build up fellow believers ``f10!}, that sincerity of\index{Heart:sincerity of ``f10!} heart, and conscience of\index{Believers:desire to obey God ``f10!} duty, out\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} of which, by the operation\index{Holy Spirit:operations:saving ``f10!} of the Spirit, this assurance may, in due time, be revived\index{Assurance:revived ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Job 13:15\index{18 Job:ch.  13, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 73:15\index{19 Psalms:ch.  73, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 50:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  50, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and by the which, in the mean time, they are supported from\index{Assurance:Holy Spirit keeps believer from utter despair ``f10!} utter despair\index{despair ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Micah 7:7\index{33 Micah:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{33 Micah:ch.   7, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; \section{Chapter 19 -- Of the Law of God} 19.1\ \ God gave to Adam a law\index{Adam:given a law ``f10!}, as a covenant of works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!}, by which He bound him and all his posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} to personal, entire, exact, and perpetual obedience\index{Covenant:works:perpetual obedience required ``f10!}; promised life\index{Covenant:first:promised life ``f10!} upon the fulfilling, and\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!} threatened death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!} upon the breach of it\index{God's law:breach:death threatened ``f10!}: and endued him\index{Mankind:created:attributes ``f10!} with power and ability to keep\index{Covenant:works:Adam:original ability and power to keep ``f10!} it.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!} with Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 19, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; Job 28:28\index{18 Job:ch.  28, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.2\ \ This law, after his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, continued to be a perfect rule of righteousness, and, as\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} such, was delivered by\index{God's law:commandments:delivered on Sinai ``f10!} God upon Mount Sinai\index{Sinai, mount ``f10!}, in ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments, and written in two tables\index{God's law:commandments:two tables ``f10!}:\footnote{\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{, 10-12}\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.   8, 10-12, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.   4, pg. ``f30!} the four first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}s\index{God's law:commandments:first four, duty to God ``f10!} containing our duty towards\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} God; and the other six\index{Sabbath:six days:for own affairs ``f10!} our duty to man\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:37-40\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  37-40, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.3\ \ Beside this law, commonly called moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}, God was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to give to the people of Israel\index{Israel ``f10!}, as a church\index{Church:OT ``f10!} under age, ceremonial\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} laws, containing several typical\index{types, OT ``f10!} ordinances, partly\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:signified Christ ``f10!} of worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}, prefiguring\index{Jesus:prefigured in ceremonial ordinances ``f10!} Christ, His graces\index{Jesus:full of grace ``f10!}, actions, sufferings, and\index{Jesus:death:sufferings and death ``f10!} benefits;\footnote{\ Hebrews chap. 9; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:1-3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} and partly holding\index{God's law:benefits ``f10!} forth divers instructions of moral duties.\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 6:17\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 23\index{65 Jude:v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} All which ceremonial laws are now abrogated\index{Ceremonial law:abrogated ``f10!}, under the new testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Colossians 2:14, 16-17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  14, 16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 9:27\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.4\ \ To them also, as a body politic, He gave sundry judicial laws, which expired\index{God's law:judicial:expired ``f10!} together with the State of that people; not obliging any other now, further than the general equity thereof\index{God's law:judicial:apply equity today ``f10!} may require.\footnote{\ Exodus chap. 21; Exodus 22:1-29\index{02 Exodus:ch.  22, v.   1-29, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 49:10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  49, v.  10, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:38-39\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 9:8-10\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   9, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.5\ \ The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law does for ever bind all\index{God's law:binding on all men ``f10!}, as well justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!} persons as others, to the obedience thereof\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 13:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4, 7-8\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3-4, 7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} and that, not only in regard of the matter contained in it, but also in respect of the authority of God the Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things ``f10!}, who gave it:\footnote{\ James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} neither does Christ, in the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, any way dissolve, but much strengthen this obligation\index{God's law:obligation to obey:strengthened by Gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:8\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:31\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.6\ \ Although true believers\index{Covenant:works:believers not under ``f10!} be not under the law, as a covenant of works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!}, to be thereby justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!}, or condemned\index{Covenant:works:believers delivered from ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:3\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}9\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} yet is it of great use to them, as well as to others; in that, as a rule of life\index{God's law:moral:rule for life ``f10!} informing them of the will of God, and their duty, it\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} directs, and binds them\index{God's law:binding on all men ``f10!} to walk accordingly;\footnote{\ Romans 7:12\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}, 22, 25\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, 22, 25, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:4-6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:19\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4, 16, 18-23\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  14, 16, 18-23, pg. ``f30!}.} discovering also the sinful pollutions\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:polluted ``f10!} of their nature, hearts, and lives\index{Heart:polluted ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 7:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} so as, examining\index{God's law:examine self against ``f10!} themselves thereby, they may come to further conviction\index{God's law:conviction of sin furthered ``f10!} of, humiliation for\index{Humility:before God ``f10!}, and hatred against\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} sin;\footnote{\ James 1:23-25\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  23-25, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:9, 14, 24\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   9, 14, 24, pg. ``f30!}.} together with a clearer sight of the need they have of Christ, and the perfection of His obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}.\footnote{\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!} It is likewise of use to the regenerate\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}, to restrain their corruptions, in\index{God's law:restrains corruptions ``f10!} that it forbids\index{God's law:forbids sin ``f10!} sin:\footnote{\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 101, 104, 128, pg. ``f30!} of it serve to show what even their sins deserve\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!}; and what afflictions, in\index{God's law:breach:define afflictions imposed on sin ``f10!} this life, they may expect for them, although freed\index{Believers:freed from:curse of the law ``f10!} from the curse thereof\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!} threatened in\index{God's law:commandments:threatenings for disobedience ``f10!} the law.\footnote{\ Ezra 9:13-14\index{15 Ezra:ch.   9, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 89:30-34\index{19 Psalms:ch.  89, v.  30-34, pg. ``f30!}.} The promises\index{God's law:promises ``f10!} of it, in like manner, show them God's approbation\index{God's law:approbation for obedience ``f10!} of obedience, and\index{Believers:obedience:rewarded ``f10!} what blessings they\index{Believers:blessed in/by God ``f10!} may expect upon the performance thereof;\footnote{\ Leviticus 26:1-14\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  26, v.   1-14, pg. ``f30!} with 2 Corinthians 6:16\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 37:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  37, v.  11, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:5\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} although not as due to them by the law, as a covenant of works.\footnote{\ Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} So as, a man's doing good, and refraining from evil\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:refraining from evil ``f10!}, because the law encourages to the one and deterrers\index{God's law:deterrence from sin ``f10!} from the other, is no evidence of his being under the law; and not under grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 6:12, 14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:8-12\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   8-12, pg. ``f30!} with Psalm 34:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2-16\index{19 Psalms:ch.  34, v.  12-16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
19.7\ \ Neither are the forementioned uses of the law contrary to the grace of\index{Grace:of Gospel ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, but do sweetly comply\index{God's law:compliance with help of Holy Spirit ``f10!} with it;\footnote{\ Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!} subduing and\index{Holy Spirit:subdues will of man ``f10!} enabling the\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} will of man to do that, freely\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!} and cheerfully\index{cheerfulness ``f10!}, which the will of God, revealed in the law\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!}, requires to be\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} done.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 8:10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   8, v.  10, pg. ``f30!} with Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 20 -- Of Christian Liberty, and Liberty of Conscience} \index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!}\index{Conscience:liberty of:defined ``f10!}20.1\ \ The liberty which\index{Christian liberty:purchased by Christ ``f10!} Christ has purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!} for believers under\index{Christian liberty:believers under the Gospel ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} consists in their freedom\index{Believers:freed from:guilt of sin ``f10!} from the guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} of sin, and condemning\index{Punishment:condemnation ``f10!} wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}, the curse of the\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!} moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law;\footnote{\ Titus 2:14\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 1:10\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and, in their being delivered from this\index{Believers:delivered from:this evil world ``f10!} present evil\index{Christian liberty:deliverance from evil world ``f10!} world, bondage to Satan\index{Satan:bondage to ``f10!}, and dominion of sin\index{Christian liberty:dominion of sin destroyed ``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 1:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} from the evil of afflictions, the\index{Salvation:release from evil afflictions ``f10!} sting of death\index{Death:believers:delivered from sting of ``f10!}, the victory of\index{Death:defeated by Christ ``f10!} the grave, and everlasting\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!} damnation;\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:71\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  71, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:54-57\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  54-57, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} as also, in their free access to God\index{Believers:access to God only through Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} and their yielding\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} obedience unto Him, not out of slavish\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:not of slavish fear ``f10!} fear, but\index{Fear:slavish ``f10!} a child-like\index{Love toward God:childlike ``f10!} love and willing mind.\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:willing mind ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 4:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} All which were common also to believers under\index{Christian liberty:believers under the law ``f10!} the law.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   9, 14, pg. ``f30!}.} But, under the new testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, the liberty of Christians\index{Christian liberty:enlarged under NT economy ``f10!} is further enlarged, in their\index{Believers:freed from:yoke of the law ``f10!} freedom from the yoke\index{Ceremonial law:yoke ``f10!} of the ceremonial\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} law, to which the Jewish\index{Church:Jewish ``f10!} Church was subjected\index{Ceremonial law:subjected Jewish Church ``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 4:1-3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}, 6-7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:10-11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} and in greater boldness\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} of access to the\index{Believers:bold access to God's throne ``f10!} throne of grace\index{Grace:throne of ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:14, 16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  14, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9-22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  19-22, pg. ``f30!}.} and in fuller communications of the free Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:instructs the elect ``f10!} of God, than believers under the law did ordinarily partake\index{Believers:benefits:in this life ``f10!} of.\footnote{\ John 7:38-39\index{43 John:ch.   7, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:13, 17-18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  13, 17-18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
20.2\ \ God alone is Lord of the conscience\index{Conscience:God alone lord of ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 4:12\index{59 James:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 14:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and has left it free from the doctrines\index{Doctrine:false:of men ``f10!} and commandments\index{Commandments of men:false ``f10!} of men, which are in any thing contrary to His Word; or beside it, in matters of faith\index{Faith:contrary opinions to the ``f10!} or worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 4:19\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 5:2\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:23\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 23:8-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:24\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} So that, to believe such doctrines, or to obey such commands, out of conscience\index{Conscience:influenced falsely by others ``f10!},\footnote{\ Colossians 2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0, 22-23\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  20, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Hosea 5:11\index{28 Hosea:ch.   5, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 13:12, 16-17\index{66 Revelation:ch.  13, v.  12, 16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 8:9\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   8, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
20.3\ \ They who, upon pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of Christian liberty\index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!}, do practice any sin, or cherish any lust\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!}, do thereby destroy the\index{Conscience:liberty of:destroyed ``f10!} end of Christian liberty, which is, that being delivered out\index{Believers:delivered from:hands of enemies ``f10!} of the hands of our enemies\index{Enemies:believers delivered from ``f10!}, we might serve the\index{Love toward God:in service ``f10!} Lord, without fear\index{Fear:none ``f10!}, in holiness and\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} righteousness before\index{Believers:to serve God in righteousness ``f10!} Him, all the days of our life.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:16\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 2:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:34\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:74-75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  74-75, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
20.4\ \ And because the powers which God has ordained, and\index{Civil magistrate:ordained by God ``f10!} the liberty which\index{Christian liberty:purchased by Christ ``f10!} Christ has purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!}, are not intended by God to destroy\index{Conscience:liberty of:destroyed ``f10!}, but mutually to uphold and\index{Christian liberty:upholds just laws of men ``f10!} preserve one\index{Human life:preservation ``f10!} another; they who, upon pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of Christian liberty\index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!}, shall oppose\index{Liberty:not oppose lawful governance ``f10!} any lawful power, or the lawful exercise of it, whether it be civil or ecclesiastical\index{Church government:ecclesiastical powers not to be resisted ``f10!}, resist the ordinance of\index{Worship:ordinances:to be:esteemed ``f10!} God.\footnote{\ Matthew 12:25\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; or, to the power of godliness\index{God's attributes:power of godliness ``f10!}; or, such erroneous\index{Falsehood:false opinions ``f10!} opinions or practices, as either in their own nature, or in the manner of publishing or maintaining them, are destructive\index{Heresy:heresies ``f10!} to the external\index{Heresy:destructive or external peace of Church ``f10!} peace and order\index{Church:to maintain peace and order ``f10!} which Christ has established\index{Church:order established by Christ ``f10!} in the Church, they\index{Church:institution ``f10!} may lawfully be\index{Church discipline:heresies lawfully censured ``f10!} called to account, and proceeded against by the censures of\index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!} the Church,\footnote{\ Romans 1:32\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  32, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Corinthians 5:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 5, 11, 13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, 5, 11, 13, pg. ``f30!}; \section{Chapter 21 -- Of Religious Worship and the Sabbath Day} \index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!}\index{Worship:on the Sabbath ``f10!}\index{Sabbath:for worship ``f10!}21.1\ \ The light of nature shows\index{Revelation:natural:declares there is a God ``f10!} that there is a God, who has lordship\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} and sovereignty over all, is good, and does good unto all, and is therefore to be feared\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!}, loved\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!}, praised\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!}, called upon, trusted\index{trust in God ``f10!} in, and served\index{Love toward God:in service ``f10!}, with all the heart, and with all the soul\index{Love toward God:with all our:soul ``f10!}, and with all the might.\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:68\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  68, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 10:7\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 31:23\index{19 Psalms:ch.  31, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 18:3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  18, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 62:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  62, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 24:14\index{06 Joshua:ch.  24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 12:33\index{41 Mark:ch.  12, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} But the acceptable way of worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}ping the true God is instituted by Himself\index{Worship:correct:instituted by God ``f10!}, and so limited\index{Worship:only acts approved by God ``f10!} by His own revealed will\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!}, that He may not be worshipped according to the imaginations and\index{Worship:false:imaginations and devices of men ``f10!} devices of men, or the suggestions of Satan\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!}, under any visible\index{Idolatry:worship of likeness of any created thing ``f10!} representation\index{Idolatry:any visible representation of God or gods ``f10!}, or any other way not prescribed in the holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} Scripture.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 12:32\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  12, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:9-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 4:15-20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  15-20, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 20:4-6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
21.2\ \ Religious\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} worship is to\index{Worship:of Trinity ``f10!} be given to God, the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}; and to Him alone;\footnote{\ Matthew 4:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!} with John 5:23\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!} and 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} not to angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}, saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, or any other creature\index{creatures ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Colossians 2:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 19:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.  19, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:25\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} and since the fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, not without a Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}; nor in the mediation of any other but of Christ alone.\footnote{\ John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
21.3\ \ Prayer, with\index{Prayer:with thanksgiving ``f10!} thanksgiving\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}, being one special part of religious worship,\index{Worship:elements ``f10!}\footnote{\ Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} is by God required of all men:\footnote{\ Psalm 65:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  65, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and that it may be accepted, it is to be made in\index{Prayer:accepted in Christ ``f10!} the name of the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 14:13-14\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; \bigskip

\bigskip

\bigskip
21.6\ \ Neither prayer\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!}, nor any other part of religious worship,\index{Worship:elements ``f10!} is now under the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} either tied unto, or made more acceptable by any place in which it is performed, or towards which it is directed:\footnote{\ John 4:21\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} but God is to be worshipped everywhere\index{Worship:in spirit and truth ``f10!},\footnote{\ Malachi 1:11\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Job 1:5\index{18 Job:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 6:18, 20\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.   6, v.  18, 20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:7\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 10:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} daily,\index{Prayer:daily in private families, ``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and in secret each\index{Prayer:secret ``f10!} one by himself;\footnote{\ Matthew 6:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} so, more solemnly, in\index{Prayer:solemn ``f10!} the public assemblies, which\index{Worship:assemblies not to be neglected ``f10!} are not carelessly or wilfully to be neglected, or forsaken, when\index{Worship:not to be:forsaken ``f10!} God, by His Word or providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, calls thereunto\index{Worship:assembly called together ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 56:6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 1:20-21, 24\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   1, v.  20-21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 8:34\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   8, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:42\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:16\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
21.7\ \ As it is the law of nature, that, in general, a due proportion\index{Sabbath:proportion of time set apart for worship ``f10!} of time be set apart for the worship of God; so\index{Worship:times of ``f10!}, in His Word, by a positive\index{Sabbath:positive, moral, perpetual command ``f10!}, moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}, and perpetual commandment\index{Sabbath:perpetual commandment ``f10!}, binding all\index{Sabbath:binding on all men ``f10!} men, in all ages, He has particularly appointed one day in seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}, for a Sabbath, to\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!} be kept holy\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} unto Him:\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 56:2, 4, 6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v.   2, 4, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} which, from the beginning of the world to the resurrection of Christ\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}, was the last day of\index{Sabbath:last day of week ``f10!} the week; and, from the resurrection of Christ, was changed into the first day\index{Sabbath:first day of week ``f10!} of the week,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 16:1-2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:7\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} which, in Scripture, is\index{Sabbath:Lord's Day ``f10!} called the Lord's Day,\footnote{\ Revelation 1:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and is to be continued to the end of the world, as the Christian Sabbath\index{Sabbath:Christian ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
