21.8\ \ This Sabbath is\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} then kept holy unto the Lord, when men, after a due preparing\index{Heart:prepared for Sabbath ``f10!} of their hearts, and ordering of the\index{Church councils:directions for ordering public worship ``f10!}ir common affairs beforehand\index{Sabbath:order common affairs before ``f10!}, do not only observe an holy rest, all the day, from their own works\index{Sabbath:cease:own works ``f10!}, words, and thoughts about\index{Sabbath:avoid unnecessary, worldly thoughts ``f10!} their worldly employments and recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments and recreations ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 16:23\index{02 Exodus:ch.  16, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}, 25-26, 29-30\index{02 Exodus:ch.  16, v.  23, 25-26, 29-30, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 31:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15-19, 21-22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15-19, 21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} but also are taken up the whole time in the public and private exercises\index{Worship:private exercises ``f10!} of His worship, and in\index{Worship:of God ``f10!} the duties of necessity and\index{Sabbath:works of necessity and mercy ``f10!} mercy.\footnote{\ Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:1-13\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.   1-13, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 22 -- Of Lawful Oaths and Vows} \index{Oaths and Vows:lawful ``f10!}\index{Oaths and Vows:vows ``f10!}22.1\ \ A lawful\index{Oaths and Vows:lawful ``f10!} oath\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths ``f10!} is a part of religious worship,\index{Worship:elements ``f10!}\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 10:20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} wherein, upon just occasion, the person swearing\index{Oaths and Vows:swear only by God's name ``f10!} solemnly calls God\index{Oaths and Vows:solemnly calls God to witness ``f10!} to witness what he asserts\index{Oaths and Vows:assertion with God as witness ``f10!}, or promises\index{Oaths and Vows:promises made ``f10!}, and to judge him according to the truth or\index{Oaths and Vows:assertion of truth ``f10!} falsehood\index{Oaths and Vows:consistent with truth or falsehood ``f10!} of what he swears.\footnote{\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.   6, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}   
\bigskip
22.2\ \ The name of God only is that by which men ought to swear\index{Oaths and Vows:swear only by God's name ``f10!}; and therein it is to be used with all holy\index{God's name:holy ``f10!} fear and\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!} reverence.\footnote{\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!} rashly\index{rashness ``f10!}, by that glorious and\index{God's name:glorious and dreadful ``f10!} dreadful Name; or, to swear at all by any other thing, is sinful, and to be abhorred.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 5:7\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:34, 37\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  34, 37, pg. ``f30!}; James 5:12\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} Yet, as in matters of weight and moment, an oath\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths ``f10!} is warranted\index{Oaths and Vows:warranted by the Word of God ``f10!} by the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}, under the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, as well as under the Old;\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:23\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 65:16\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  65, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} so a lawful\index{Oaths and Vows:lawful ``f10!} oath, being imposed by lawful authority, in such matters ought to be taken.\footnote{\ I Kings 8:31; Nehemiah 13:25\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Ezra 10:5\index{15 Ezra:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
22.3\ \ Whosoever takes an oath\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths ``f10!} ought duly to consider the weightiness\index{Oaths and Vows:consider the weightiness ``f10!} of so solemn an\index{Oaths and Vows:solemn act ``f10!} act; and therein to avouch\index{Oaths and Vows:avouch only truth ``f10!} nothing, but what he is fully persuaded is the truth\index{Oaths and Vows:assertion of truth ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 4:2\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} Neither may any man bind himself\index{Oaths and Vows:bind:only to good and just ``f10!} by oath to anything but what is good and just, and what he believes so to be, and what he is able and resolved to\index{Oaths and Vows:resolve to perform ``f10!} perform.\footnote{\ Genesis 24:2-3, 5-6, 8-9\index{01 Genesis:ch.  24, v.   2-3, 5-6, 8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} Yet is it a sin to refuse\index{Oaths and Vows:not to:refuse lawful ``f10!} an oath touching anything that is good and just, being imposed by lawful authority\index{Oaths and Vows:lawful ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Numbers 5:19, 21\index{04 Numbers:ch.   5, v.  19, 21, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 5:12\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 22:7-11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  22, v.   7-11, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
22.4\ \ An oath\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths ``f10!} is to be taken in the plain and\index{Oaths and Vows:take in plain and common sense of words ``f10!} common sense of the words, without equivocation\index{Oaths and Vows:not with equivocation ``f10!}, or mental reservation\index{Oaths and Vows:no mental reservations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Jeremiah 4:2\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 24:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  24, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} It cannot oblige to sin: but in anything not sinful, being taken, it binds to\index{Oaths and Vows:bind:performance ``f10!} performance, although to a man's own hurt.\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 25:22, 32-34\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  25, v.  22, 32-34, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 15:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} Not is it to be violated\index{Oaths and Vows:not to:be violated ``f10!}, although made to heretics\index{heretics ``f10!}, or infidels\index{Oaths and Vows:to be kept, even if made to infidels ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 17:16, 18-19\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  17, v.  16, 18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 9:18-19\index{06 Joshua:ch.   9, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!} with 2 Samuel 21:1\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  21, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
22.5\ \ A vow is\index{Oaths and Vows:vow defined ``f10!} of the like nature with a promissory\index{Oaths and Vows:promissory ``f10!} oath\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths ``f10!}, and ought to be made with the like religious care\index{Oaths and Vows:religious worship ``f10!}, and to be performed with the like faithfulness\index{faithfulness ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 19:21\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  19, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 5:4-6\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 61:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  61, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 66:13-14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  66, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
22.6\ \ It is not to be made to any creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, but to God alone:\footnote{\ Psalm 76:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  76, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 44:25-26\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  44, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}.} and that it may be accepted, it is to be made voluntarily\index{Oaths and Vows:voluntary to be accepted ``f10!}, out of faith\index{Faith:when making oath or vow ``f10!}, and conscience of\index{Believers:desire to obey God ``f10!} duty, in way of thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!} for mercy received\index{Mercy:thankfulness for ``f10!}, or for the obtaining\index{Prayer:faith for obtaining wants ``f10!} of what we want; whereby we more strictly bind ourselves\index{Oaths and Vows:bind:only to good and just ``f10!} to necessary duties\index{Oaths and Vows:bind:only to necessary duties ``f10!}; or to other things, so far and so long as they may fitly conduce thereunto.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 23:21-23\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  23, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 50:14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 28:20\index{01 Genesis:ch.  28, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{01 Genesis:ch.  28, v.  20-22, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 1:11\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 66:13-14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  66, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 132:2-5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 132, v.   2-5, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
22.7\ \ No man may vow to do anything forbidden\index{Oaths and Vows:not for things:forbidden by Word of God ``f10!} in the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}, or what would hinder any\index{Oaths and Vows:bind:only to good and just ``f10!} duty therein\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} commanded, or\index{God's law:commandments:duties:not to hinder ``f10!} which is not in his own power\index{Oaths and Vows:not for things:not in person's power ``f10!}, and for the performance whereof he has no promise of ability\index{Oaths and Vows:not for things:unable to perform ``f10!} from God.\footnote{\ Acts 23:12, 14\index{44 Acts:ch.  23, v.  12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 6:26\index{41 Mark:ch.   6, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Numbers 30:5, 8, 12-13\index{04 Numbers:ch.  30, v.   5, 8, 12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} In which respects, Popish\index{Popish rituals ``f10!} monastical\index{Oaths and Vows:not to:be Popish monastical ``f10!} vows of perpetual single\index{Oaths and Vows:not to:perpetual single life ``f10!} life, professed poverty\index{Oaths and Vows:not to:professed poverty ``f10!}, and regular obedience\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!}, are so far from being degrees\index{Oaths and Vows:none of higher degrees ``f10!} of higher perfection, that\index{perfectionism ``f10!} they are superstitious\index{Superstitions:superstitions ``f10!} and sinful snares, in which no Christian may entangle himself.\footnote{\ Matthew 19:11-12\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:2, 9\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   2, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:28\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 4:2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:23\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 23 -- Of the Civil Magistrate} \index{Civil magistrate:office of ``f10!}23.1\ \ God, the supreme\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} Lord and King\index{Jesus:King ``f10!} of all the world, has ordained\index{Civil magistrate:ordained by God ``f10!} civil magistrates, to be, under Him, over the people, for His own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, and the public good: and, to this end, has armed them with the power of the sword\index{Civil magistrate:power of sword ``f10!}, for the defence\index{Civil magistrate:to defend citizens ``f10!} and encouragement of\index{Civil magistrate:to encourage those doing good ``f10!} them that are good, and for the punishment\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!} of evil doers\index{Civil magistrate:to punish evil doers ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
23.2\ \ It is lawful for Christians\index{Civil magistrate:lawful for Christians to execute office ``f10!} to accept and execute the office of a magistrate, when called thereunto;\footnote{\ Proverbs 8:15-16\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   8, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 2, 4\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, 2, 4, pg. ``f30!}.} in the managing whereof, as they ought especially to maintain piety, justice\index{Civil magistrate:to maintain justice ``f10!}, and peace, according\index{Civil magistrate:to maintain peace:in society ``f10!} to the wholesome\index{Commandments of men:wholesome ``f10!} laws of each commonwealth\index{commonwealth ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 2:10-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 82:3-4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  82, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 23:3\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  23, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} so for that end, they may lawfully now\index{war, just, lawful ``f10!}, under the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, wage war, upon just and necessary occasion.\footnote{\ Luke 3:14\index{42 Luke:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 8:9-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   8, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 10:1-2\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 17:14, 16\index{66 Revelation:ch.  17, v.  14, 16, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
23.3\ \ The civil magistrate may not assume to himself the administration\index{Civil magistrate:not to administer word or sacraments ``f10!} of the Word and sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, or the power\index{Church:power delegated by Christ ``f10!} of the keys\index{Kingdom:keys of ``f10!} of the kingdom of heaven\index{Kingdom:of heaven ``f10!}:\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 26:18\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  26, v.  18, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 18:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!} and Matthew 16:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  16, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 4:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} yet he has authority, and it is his duty, to take order, that unity\index{Civil magistrate:to ensure unity and peace in Church ``f10!} and peace be\index{Civil magistrate:to maintain peace:in Church ``f10!} preserved in the Church, that\index{Church:institution ``f10!} the truth of God be\index{Truth:to be kept pure by civil magistrate ``f10!} kept pure and entire; that\index{Civil magistrate:to keep truth of God pure ``f10!} all blasphemies\index{blasphemy ``f10!} and heresies\index{Heresy:heresies ``f10!} be suppressed\index{Civil magistrate:to suppress blasphemies and heresies ``f10!}; all corruptions and\index{Worship:false:corruptions in ``f10!} abuses\index{Worship:not to be:abused ``f10!} in worship and\index{Worship:abuses ``f10!} discipline\index{Church discipline:discipline ``f10!} prevented\index{Civil magistrate:to keep worship of God pure ``f10!} or reformed; and all the ordinances of God duly\index{Civil magistrate:to ensure ordinances of God administrated ``f10!} settled, administrated, and observed.\footnote{\ Isaiah 49:23\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  49, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 122:9\index{19 Psalms:ch. 122, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Ezra 7:23, 25-28\index{15 Ezra:ch.   7, v.  23, 25-28, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 24:16\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  24, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 13:5-6, 12\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  13, v.   5-6, 12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 18:4\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  18, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Chronicles 13:1-9\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  13, v.   1-9, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 23:1-26\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  23, v.   1-26, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 34:33\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  34, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 15:12-13\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  15, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} For the better effecting whereof, he has power\index{Civil magistrate:to call synods to consult and advise ``f10!} to call synods\index{Church government:synods ``f10!}, to be present at them, and to provide that whatsoever is transacted in them be according to the mind of God.\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 19:8-11\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  19, v.   8-11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 29; 2 Chronicles 30; Matthew 2:4-5\index{40 Matthew:ch.   2, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the }\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription }}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Clarifications}}\textcolor{black}{).}}   
\bigskip
23.4\ \ It is the duty of people\index{Prayer:for magistrates ``f10!} to pray for magistrates\index{Civil magistrate:pray for ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} to honour their\index{Civil magistrate:to be honoured ``f10!} persons,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:17\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} to pay them tribute\index{Civil magistrate:to be paid tribute and dues ``f10!} or other dues,\footnote{\ Romans 13:6-7\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} to obey their\index{Commandments of men:lawful to be obeyed ``f10!} lawful commands, and to be subject to their authority, for conscience\index{Conscience:for sake of ``f10!}{}' sake.\footnote{\ Romans 13:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:1\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} Infidelity\index{Civil magistrate:legal authority even if:infidels ``f10!}, or difference in religion, does\index{Civil magistrate:legal authority even if:different religion ``f10!} not make void the magistrates' just and legal\index{Civil magistrate:legal authority even if:unbelievers ``f10!} authority, nor free the people from their due obedience to them:\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}, 16\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, 16, pg. ``f30!}.} from which ecclesiastical\index{Church officers:to obey legal laws of civil authorities ``f10!} persons are not exempted,\footnote{\ Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 2:35\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   2, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 25:9-11\index{44 Acts:ch.  25, v.   9-11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 2:1, 10-11\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   2, v.   1, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 8-11\index{65 Jude:v. 8-11, pg. ``f30!}.} much less has the Pope\index{Pope:of Rome ``f10!} any power and jurisdiction\index{Civil magistrate:pope has no jurisdiction over ``f10!} over them in their dominions\index{Pope:no jurisdiction over people in their dominions ``f10!}, or over any of their people; and, least of all, to deprive them of their dominions, or lives, if he shall judge the\index{Jesus:judge:world ``f10!}m\index{Pope:not to judge magistrates as heretics ``f10!} to be heretics\index{heretics ``f10!}, or upon any other pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} whatsoever.\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 2:4\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 13:15-17\index{66 Revelation:ch.  13, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 24 -- Of Marriage and Divorce} \index{Marriage:Biblical definition ``f10!}\index{Divorce:divorce ``f10!}24.1\ \ Marriage\index{Marriage:Biblical definition ``f10!} is to be between one man and one woman: neither is it lawful for any\index{Polygamy:unlawful ``f10!} man to have more than one wife\index{Marriage:one spouse ``f10!}, nor for any woman to have more than one husband; at the same time.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:24\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 19:5\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 2:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
24.2\ \ Marriage\index{Marriage:Biblical definition ``f10!} was ordained for the mutual help\index{Marriage:mutual help ``f10!} of husband and wife,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:18\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} for the increase of mankind with\index{Marriage:to increase mankind ``f10!} a legitimate\index{Marriage:to produce legitimate issue (offspring) ``f10!} issue, and of the Church with\index{Church:home of believers ``f10!} an holy seed\index{Marriage:produce holy seed for Church ``f10!};\footnote{\ Malachi 2:15\index{39 Malachi:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and for preventing of uncleanness\index{Marriage:to prevent uncleanness ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:2, 9\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   2, 9, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
24.3\ \ It is lawful for all\index{Marriage:lawful:for all ``f10!} sorts of people to marry, who are able with judgment to\index{Judgement:temporal ``f10!} give their consent\index{Marriage:consent of parties ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 4:3\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:36-38\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  36-38, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 24:57-58\index{01 Genesis:ch.  24, v.  57-58, pg. ``f30!}.} Yet is it the duty of Christians to marry only\index{Marriage:Christians:only in the Lord ``f10!} in the Lord:\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:39\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} and therefore such as profess the true\index{Profession:of true religion ``f10!} reformed religion should not marry with\index{Marriage:Christians:not with infidels or papists ``f10!} infidels, papists\index{papists ``f10!}, or other idolaters\index{Idolatry:idolatry ``f10!}: neither should such as are godly be unequally yoked\index{Marriage:not unequally yoked ``f10!}, by marrying with such as are notoriously\index{Marriage:not with notoriously wicked ``f10!} wicked in their life, or maintain damnable heresies\index{Heresy:heresies ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 34:14\index{01 Genesis:ch.  34, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 34:1\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 7:3-4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   7, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; I Kings 11:4; Nehemiah 13:25\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26, 27\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  25-26, 27, pg. ``f30!}; Malachi 2:11-12\index{39 Malachi:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 6:14\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}    
\bigskip
24.4\ \ Marriage\index{Marriage:Biblical definition ``f10!} ought not to be within the degrees of consanguinity\index{Consanguinity:consanguinity ``f10!} or affinity forbidden\index{Consanguinity:forbidden affinity ``f10!} by the Word;\footnote{\ Leviticus 18; 1 Corinthians 5:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 2:7\index{30 Amos:ch.   2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} nor can such incestuous marriages\index{Marriage:unlawful ``f10!} ever be made lawful by any\index{Consanguinity:incestuous marriage not lawful ``f10!} law of man or consent of parties\index{Marriage:consent of parties ``f10!}, so as those persons may live together as man and wife\index{Marriage:live together as man and wife ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Mark 6:18\index{41 Mark:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 18:24-28\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  18, v.  24-28, pg. ``f30!}.} The man may not marry any\index{Marriage:not near kindred of wife ``f10!} of his wife's kindred\index{Consanguinity:near kindred ``f10!} nearer in blood\index{Consanguinity:nearness of blood ``f10!} than he may of his own; nor the woman of her husband's kindred nearer in blood than of her own.\footnote{\ Leviticus 20:19-21\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  20, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the }\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription }}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Exceptions}}\textcolor{black}{).} }   
\bigskip
24.5\ \ Adultery\index{Sexual immorality:adultery ``f10!} or fornication\index{Sexual immorality:fornication ``f10!} committed after a contract\index{Contracts:marriage ``f10!}, being detected\index{Marriage:valid reasons for ending ``f10!} before marriage, gives just occasion to the innocent party to dissolve that contract.\footnote{\ Matthew 1:18-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.   1, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}.} In the case of adultery after marriage, it is lawful for the innocent party to sue out a divorce\index{Divorce:divorce ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Matthew 5:31-32\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  31-32, pg. ``f30!}.} and, after the divorce, to marry another\index{Marriage:remarriage permitted for innocent party after divorce ``f10!}, as if the offending\index{Divorce:offending treated as dead ``f10!} party were dead\index{Death:divorced marriage partner viewed as dead ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 19:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:2-3\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
24.6\ \ Although the corruption of man\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} be such as is apt to study arguments unduly to put asunder\index{Marriage:not to be broken, except if adultery ``f10!} those whom God has joined together in marriage: yet nothing but adultery\index{Sexual immorality:adultery ``f10!}, or such wilful desertion\index{Marriage:desertion ``f10!} as can no way be remedied by the Church or\index{Church:institution ``f10!} civil magistrate, is\index{Civil magistrate:role in divorce cases ``f10!} cause sufficient of dissolving\index{Marriage:valid reasons for ending ``f10!} the bond of marriage:\footnote{\ Matthew 19:8-9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:15\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 19:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} wherein, a public and orderly course of proceeding is to be observed; and the persons concerned in it not left to their own wills and\index{Causation:will of creatures:not to be exercised to dissolve marriage ``f10!} discretion, in their own case.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 24:1-4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  24, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 25 -- Of the Church} \index{Church:institution ``f10!}25.1\ \ The catholic\index{Church:catholic ``f10!} or universal Church\index{Church:universal ``f10!} which is invisible, consists\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} of the whole number of the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}, that have been, are, or shall be gathered into one, under Christ the Head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} thereof; and is the spouse\index{Church:Christ's spouse ``f10!}, the body, the fulness of Him\index{Jesus:fulness of all things ``f10!} that fills\index{Jesus:fills all in all ``f10!} all in all.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0, 22-23\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  10, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}, 27, 32\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, 27, 32, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
25.2\ \ The visible Church\index{Church:visible ``f10!}, which is also catholic\index{Church:catholic ``f10!} or universal under\index{Church:universal ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} (not confined to one nation as\index{Gospel:to all nations ``f10!} before under the law), consists of all those throughout the world that profess the true\index{Profession:of true religion ``f10!} religion;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:12-13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 2:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 7:9\index{66 Revelation:ch.   7, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 15:9, 10-12\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   9, 10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and of their children:\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 16:20-21\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  16, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:16\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:15\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} and is the kingdom of the\index{Kingdom:of Christ ``f10!} Lord Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ Matthew 13:47\index{40 Matthew:ch.  13, v.  47, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 9:7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} the house and\index{Church:home of believers ``f10!} family of\index{Church:family of God ``f10!} God,\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:15\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} out of which there is no ordinary\index{Church:ordinary means of salvation ``f10!} possibility of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 2:47\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  47, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
25.3\ \ Unto this catholic\index{Church:catholic ``f10!} visible Church\index{Church:visible ``f10!} Christ has given the ministry\index{Church:given the ministry of God ``f10!}, oracles\index{Church:endowed with oracles of God ``f10!}, and ordinances of God, for\index{Church:furnished with:ordinances of God ``f10!} the gathering\index{Church:universal ``f10!} and perfecting of\index{Church:perfecting of saints ``f10!} the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, in this life, to the end of the world: and does by His own presence and Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:works in the Church ``f10!}, according to His promise\index{Church:promised presence of God ``f10!}, make them effectual thereunto\index{Worship:ordinances:made effectual for salvation ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 12:28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11-13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
25.4\ \ This catholic\index{Church:catholic ``f10!} Church has been sometimes more, sometimes less visible.\footnote{\ Romans 11:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 12:6, 14\index{66 Revelation:ch.  12, v.   6, 14, pg. ``f30!}.} And particular Churches, which\index{Church:mix of truth and error ``f10!} are members thereof\index{Church members ``f10!}, are more or less pure\index{Church:true:marks ``f10!}, according as the doctrine of the\index{Doctrine:Gospel ``f10!} Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} is taught and\index{Gospel:to be taught and embraced ``f10!} embraced, ordinances administered, and\index{Church:true:ordinances administered ``f10!} public worship\index{Worship:public ``f10!} performed more or less purely in them.\footnote{\ Revelation 2; Revelation 3; 1 Corinthians 5:6-7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
25.5\ \ The purest Churches under\index{Church:mix of truth and error ``f10!} heaven are subject both to mixture and error:\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 13:12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 2; Revelation 3; Matthew 13:24-30, 47\index{40 Matthew:ch.  13, v.  24-30, 47, pg. ``f30!}.} and some have so degenerated\index{Church:degenerated churches ``f10!}, as to become no Churches of\index{Church:false, synagogues of Satan ``f10!} Christ, but synagogues of Satan.\footnote{\ Revelation 18:2\index{66 Revelation:ch.  18, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:18-22\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  18-22, pg. ``f30!}.} Nevertheless, there shall be always a Church\index{Church:indestructible ``f10!} on earth, to worship God\index{Worship:always be a Church to worship ``f10!} according to His will.\footnote{\ Matthew 16:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  16, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 72:17\index{19 Psalms:ch.  72, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 102:28\index{19 Psalms:ch. 102, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
25.6\ \ There is no other head of the\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} Church, but the Lord Jesus Christ;\footnote{\ Colossians 1:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:22\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} nor can the Pope\index{Pope:of Rome ``f10!} of Rome, in any sense, be head thereof\index{Pope:not head of the Church ``f10!}; but is that Antichrist\index{Antichrist (Pope) ``f10!}, that man of sin, and son of perdition\index{Pope:son of perdition ``f10!}, that exalts\index{Pope:exalts self ``f10!} himself, in the Church, against\index{Church:institution ``f10!} Christ and all that is called God.\footnote{\ Matthew 23:8-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:3-4, 8-9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   3-4, 8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 13:6\index{66 Revelation:ch.  13, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the }\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription }}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Exceptions}}\textcolor{black}{).}}  

\section{Chapter 26 -- Of the Communion of the Saints} \index{Communion:of saints ``f10!}\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}26.1\ \ All saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, that are united to Jesus\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} Christ their Head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} by His Spirit and by faith\index{Faith:worked in believers by the Holy Spirit ``f10!}, have fellowship with\index{Fellowship:with Christ ``f10!} Him in His grace\index{Grace:fellowship with Jesus in ``f10!}, sufferings, death\index{Jesus:death:sufferings and death ``f10!}, resurrection, and glory:\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ ``f10!}\footnote{\ John 1:3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  16-19, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:10\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 2:12\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} and, being united to one\index{Believers:united to one another ``f10!} another in love, they\index{Love for others:united ``f10!} have communion\index{Communion:of saints ``f10!} in each other's gifts and graces,\index{Love for others:acknowledge gifts and graces of others ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:15-16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 3:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1-23\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:19\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and are obliged to the performance of such duties\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!}, public and private, as do conduce to their mutual good\index{Good works:for mutual good ``f10!}, both in the inward\index{Love for others:inward thoughts further others' good ``f10!} and outward man\index{Love for others:for saints ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 5:11\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  11, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:11-12, 14\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  11-12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  16-18, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 6:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   6, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
26.2\ \ Saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} by profession are\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} bound to maintain a holy\index{Worship:holy fellowship to be maintained ``f10!} fellowship and\index{Fellowship:with fellow believers ``f10!} communion in the\index{Communion:in worship ``f10!} worship of God; and in performing such other spiritual services\index{Good works:spiritual services ``f10!} as tend to their mutual edification\index{Love for others:mutual:edification ``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:24-25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, 46, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 2:3\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} as also in relieving\index{Love for others:mutual:relieving in outward things ``f10!} each other in outward things\index{Love for others:for saints ``f10!}, according to their several abilities, and necessities. Which communion, as\index{Communion:with God ``f10!} God offers\index{Church:communion with all who call upon Jesus ``f10!} opportunity\index{Communion:of saints ``f10!}, is to be extended unto all those who, in every place, call upon the name of the Lord Jesus.\footnote{\ Acts 2:44-45\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  44-45, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 8; 2 Corinthians 9; Acts 11:29-30\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  29-30, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
26.3\ \ This communion which\index{Communion:with Christ ``f10!} the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} have with Christ, does not make them, in any wise, partakers\index{Believers:union with Christ:not partakers of Godhead ``f10!} of the substance of His Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!}; or to be equal with Christ\index{Communion:with Christ, does not make believers equal to him ``f10!}, in any respect: either of which to affirm is impious and blasphemous\index{blasphemy ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Colossians 1:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 8:6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 42:8\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 45:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews 1:8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} Nor does their communion one\index{Communion:of saints ``f10!} with another, as saints, take away, or infringe\index{property, rights not to be infringed ``f10!} the title or propriety which each man has in his goods\index{Theft:infringe on property of others ``f10!} and possessions.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:28\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 5:4\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 27 -- Of the Sacraments} \index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}27.1\ \ Sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} are holy\index{Sacraments:signs and seals:holy ``f10!} signs\index{Sacraments:holy:signs ``f10!} and seals\index{Sacraments:covenant seals ``f10!} of the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 10, pg. ``f30!}.} immediately instituted by God\index{Sacraments:instituted by:God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} to represent Christ\index{Sacraments:represent Christ ``f10!} and His benefits; and to\index{Sacraments:benefits:worthy believers receive ``f10!} confirm\index{Sacraments:confirm union with Christ ``f10!} our interest in Him\index{Believers:interest (share) in Christ ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:17\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} as also, to put a visible\index{Sacraments:signs and seals:visible difference ``f10!} difference between those that belong unto the Church, and\index{Church:institution ``f10!} the rest of the world;\footnote{\ Romans 15:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 12:48\index{02 Exodus:ch.  12, v.  48, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 34:14\index{01 Genesis:ch.  34, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and solemnly to\index{Sacraments:solemn engagement to God's service ``f10!} engage\index{Sacraments:engage participants to service of God ``f10!} them to the service of\index{Love toward God:in service ``f10!} God in Christ, according to His Word.\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}, 21\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, 21, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
27.2\ \ There is in every sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} a spiritual relation\index{Sacraments:spiritual relation between sign and signified ``f10!}, or sacramental\index{Lord's Supper:elements:union between sign and signified ``f10!} union, between\index{Sacraments:union between sign and signified ``f10!} the sign and the thing signified: whence it comes to pass, that the names and effects of the one are attributed to the other.\footnote{\ Genesis 17:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:27-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
27.3\ \ The grace which\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments ``f10!} is exhibited in\index{Sacraments:grace:exhibited ``f10!} or by the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} rightly used\index{Sacraments:grace:conferred ``f10!}, is not conferred by any\index{Sacraments:grace:not conferred by elements ``f10!} power in them; neither does the efficacy of a\index{Sacraments:spiritual efficacy ``f10!} sacrament depend upon the piety or\index{Lord's Supper:efficacy, not dependent on piety or intention of person administering ``f10!} intention of him that does administer it:\footnote{\ Romans 2:28-29\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:21\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} but upon the work of the Spirit,\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit and the word ``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 3:11\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and the word of institution\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!}, which contains, together with a precept authorizing the use thereof, a promise of benefit to\index{Sacraments:benefits:worthy believers receive ``f10!} worthy receivers.\footnote{\ Matthew 26:27-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
27.4\ \ There are only two sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} ordained by\index{Sacraments:ordained by Jesus ``f10!} Christ our Lord in the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}; that is to say, Baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} of the Lord: neither of which may be dispensed\index{Sacraments:to be:dispensed by minister of the Word ``f10!} by any but by a minister\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of the Word lawfully\index{Preachers:to be:lawfully ordained ``f10!} ordained.\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, 23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 4:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
27.5\ \ The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}, in regard to the spiritual things\index{Sacraments:spiritual things signified, same in both Testaments ``f10!} thereby signified and exhibited, were, for substance\index{Sacraments:OT and NT same substance ``f10!}, the same with those of the New.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:1-4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 28 -- Of Baptism} \index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!}28.1\ \ Baptism is a\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, ordained by\index{Sacraments:ordained by Jesus ``f10!} Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} not only for the solemn admission\index{Baptism:admission into visible Church ``f10!} of the party baptized into the visible Church\index{Church:visible ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} but also, to be unto him a sign\index{Baptism:sign of salvation ``f10!} and seal of\index{Baptism:seal of salvationof ``f10!} the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!} with Colossians 2:11-12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} of his ingrafting\index{Believers:ingrafted into Christ ``f10!} into Christ,\footnote{\ Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} of regeneration\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!},\footnote{\ Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} of remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins ``f10!} of sins,\footnote{\ Mark 1:4\index{41 Mark:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and of his giving up unto God through Jesus Christ, to walk in the newness\index{Baptism:walk in newness of life ``f10!} of life.\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.} Which sacrament is, by Christ's own appointment, to be\index{Baptism:appointed by Christ for Church ``f10!} continued in His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!} until the end of the world.\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
28.2\ \ The outward element to be used in this sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} is water\index{Baptism:to use water ``f10!}, wherewith the party is to be baptized\index{Baptism:in name of Trinity ``f10!}, in the name of the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, and of the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, by a minister\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, lawfully call\index{Civil magistrate:to call synods to consult and advise ``f10!}ed\index{Preachers:to be:lawfully called ``f10!} thereunto.\footnote{\ Matthew 3:11\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
28.3\ \ Dipping\index{Baptism:modes:dipping ``f10!} of the person into the water is\index{Baptism:to use water ``f10!} not necessary; but Baptism is rightly administered\index{Baptism:modes:valid ``f10!} by pouring\index{Baptism:modes:pouring ``f10!} or sprinkling\index{Baptism:modes:sprinkling ``f10!} water upon the person.\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:10, 19-22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  10, 19-22, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:41\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:33\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 7:4\index{41 Mark:ch.   7, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
28.4\ \ Not only those that do actually profess faith\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} in and obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} unto Christ,\footnote{\ Mark 16:15\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 8:37-38\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.  37-38, pg. ``f30!}.} but also the infants of one\index{Infants:of believing parents, to be baptized ``f10!} or both believing\index{Baptism:infants of believing parents ``f10!} parents, are to be baptized\index{Baptism:infants ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9-10, pg. ``f30!} with Galatians 3:9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   9, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:11-12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}{}-39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!} and Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 10:13-16\index{41 Mark:ch.  10, v.  13-16, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 18:1\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
28.5\ \ Although it be a great sin to contemn\index{Baptism:not to be treated with contempt ``f10!} or neglect this\index{Baptism:not to neglect ``f10!} ordinance,\footnote{\ Luke 7:30\index{42 Luke:ch.   7, v.  30, pg. ``f30!} with Exodus 4:24-26\index{02 Exodus:ch.   4, v.  24-26, pg. ``f30!}.} yet grace\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments ``f10!} and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} are not so inseparably\index{Sanctification:inseparable from:grace ``f10!} annexed unto it, as that no person can be regenerated\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!} or saved without\index{Salvation:not without grace ``f10!} it;\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 10:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 4, 22, 31, 45, 47\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.   2, 4, 22, 31, 45, 47, pg. ``f30!}.} or, that all that are baptized\index{Baptism:not all baptized are regenerated ``f10!} are undoubtedly regenerated.\footnote{\ Acts 8:13, 23\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.  13, 23, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
28.6\ \ The efficacy\index{Baptism:spiritual efficacy ``f10!} of Baptism is not tied to that moment of\index{Baptism:efficacy not time dependent ``f10!} time wherein it is administered;\footnote{\ John 3:5\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}, 8\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   5, 8, pg. ``f30!}.} yet notwithstanding, by the right use of this ordinance\index{Baptism:ordinance, to be used rightly ``f10!}, the grace promised is\index{Baptism:means of grace ``f10!} not only offered, but really exhibited and\index{Baptism:grace:exhibited ``f10!} conferred, by\index{Baptism:grace:conferred by Holy Spirit ``f10!} the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, to such (whether of age or infants) as\index{Infants:of believing parents, to be baptized ``f10!} that grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} belongs unto, according to the counsel of God's\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will, in His appointed time.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5-26\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}, 41\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, 41, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
28.7\ \ The sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of Baptism is but\index{Baptism:to be administered once ``f10!} once to be administered unto any person.\footnote{\ Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 29 -- Of the Lord's Supper} \index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}29.1\ \ Our Lord Jesus, in the night wherein He was betrayed\index{Jesus:betrayed ``f10!}, instituted the\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of His body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!}, called the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, to be observed in\index{Lord's Supper:to be observed to end of world ``f10!} His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, unto the end of the world, for the perpetual remembrance\index{Lord's Supper:remembrance of Christ's sacrifice ``f10!} of the sacrifice of Himself\index{Jesus:sacrifice:of himself ``f10!} in His death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}; the sealing\index{Lord's Supper:benefits sealed ``f10!} all benefits thereof unto\index{Lord's Supper:benefits believers receive ``f10!} true believers, their spiritual nourishment\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:nourishment ``f10!} and growth in Him\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in Christ ``f10!}, their further engagement in and\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} to all duties which\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} they owe unto Him; and to be a bond and pledge\index{Lord's Supper:pledge of communion with Christ ``f10!} of their communion with Him, and\index{Communion:with Christ ``f10!} with each other, as members of His\index{Church members ``f10!} mystical\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} body.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-26, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}, 21\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16-17, 21, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.2\ \ In this sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, Christ is not offered up to\index{Lord's Supper:not a sacrifice:of Jesus ``f10!} His Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}; nor any real sacrifice made at all for remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins ``f10!} of sins of the quick or dead\index{Lord's Supper:not a sacrifice:for quick or dead ``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}, 25-26, 28\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  22, 25-26, 28, pg. ``f30!}.} but only a commemoration\index{Lord's Supper:commemoration ``f10!} of that one offering up of Himself\index{Jesus:sacrifice:of himself ``f10!}, by Himself, upon the cross\index{Jesus:death:on cross ``f10!}, once for all: and a spiritual oblation\index{Lord's Supper:remembrance of Christ's sacrifice ``f10!} of all possible praise unto\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} God for the same:\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-26, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} so that the Popish\index{Popish rituals ``f10!} sacrifice of the\index{Lord's Supper:not a sacrifice:of the mass ``f10!} mass\index{Mass:Roman Catholic ``f10!} (as they call it) is most abominably injurious to Christ's one, only sacrifice, the\index{Jesus:sacrifice:once only ``f10!} alone propitiation\index{Jesus:sacrifice:propitiation ``f10!} for all the sins of His elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 7:23-24, 27\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  23-24, 27, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1-12, 14, 18\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  11-12, 14, 18, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.3\ \ The Lord Jesus has, in this ordinance, appointed His ministers\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} to declare His\index{Preachers:declare word of institution at Lord's Supper ``f10!} word of institution\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!} to the people; to pray, and bless the\index{Lord's Supper:elements:Jesus blessed ``f10!} elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} of bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!}, and thereby to set them apart from a common to a holy\index{Lord's Supper:elements:holy use ``f10!} use; and to take and break the\index{Lord's Supper:bread broken ``f10!} bread, to take the cup\index{Lord's Supper:cup ``f10!}, and (they communicating\index{Lord's Supper:communion ``f10!} also themselves) to give both to the communicants\index{Lord's Supper:both bread and wine to communicants ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!} and Mark 14:22-24\index{41 Mark:ch.  14, v.  22-24, pg. ``f30!} and Luke 22:19\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-26, pg. ``f30!}.} but to none who are not then present in the congregation\index{Lord's Supper:only to those present in congregation ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts. 20:7; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} 
\bigskip
29.4\ \ Private\index{Mass:private ``f10!} masses\index{Mass:Roman Catholic ``f10!}, or receiving this\index{Lord's Supper:not private ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} by a priest or\index{Lord's Supper:not consecrated by a priest ``f10!} any other alone;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} as likewise, the denial\index{Lord's Supper:both bread and wine to communicants ``f10!} of the cup\index{Lord's Supper:cup ``f10!} to the people,\footnote{\ Mark 14:23\index{41 Mark:ch.  14, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25-29, pg. ``f30!}.} worshipping the elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!}, the lifting\index{Lord's Supper:elements:not to be lifted for adoration ``f10!} them up or carrying them about for adoration\index{Idolatry:adoration of eucharistic elements ``f10!}, and the reserving them for any pretended religious use\index{Lord's Supper:elements:not to be used incorrectly ``f10!}; are all contrary to the nature of this sacrament, and to the institution\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!} of Christ.\footnote{\ Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.5\ \ The outward elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} in this sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, duly set apart to the uses ordained by\index{Sacraments:ordained by Jesus ``f10!} Christ, have such relation to Him\index{Lord's Supper:elements:relation to Christ crucified ``f10!} crucified\index{Jesus:crucified ``f10!}, as that, truly, yet sacramentally\index{Lord's Supper:elements:union between sign and signified ``f10!} only, they are sometimes called by the name of the things they represent, to\index{Lord's Supper:elements:represent Christ ``f10!} wit, the body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!} of Christ;\footnote{\ Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!}.} albeit in substance and nature they still remain truly\index{Lord's Supper:elements:remain truly and only natural ``f10!} and only bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!}, as they were before.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:29\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.6\ \ That doctrine\index{Doctrine:false:transubstantiation ``f10!} which maintains\index{Lord's Supper:elements:transubstantiation:repugnant ``f10!} a change of the substance of bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!} into the substance of Christ's body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!} (commonly called transubstantiation\index{Lord's Supper:elements:transubstantiation:superstition ``f10!}) by consecration\index{Lord's Supper:elements:not changed by consecration of priest ``f10!} of a priest, or by\index{Lord's Supper:not consecrated by a priest ``f10!} any other way, is repugnant, not to Scripture alone, but even to common sense and reason; overthrows the nature of the sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, and has been, and is the cause of manifold superstitions\index{Superstitions:superstitions ``f10!}; yea, of gross idolatries\index{Idolatry:idolatry ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-26, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 24:6, 39\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.   6, 39, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.7\ \ Worthy\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!} receivers outwardly partaking\index{Lord's Supper:elements:outward partaking ``f10!} of the visible elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} in this sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} do then also, inwardly by faith, really and indeed, yet not carnally\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:not carnal ``f10!} and corporally\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:not corporal ``f10!}, but spiritually, receive and feed\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:in faith ``f10!} upon Christ crucified\index{Jesus:crucified ``f10!}, and all benefits of\index{Lord's Supper:benefits believers receive ``f10!} His death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}: the body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!} of Christ being then, not corporally or carnally, in, with, or under the bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!}; yet, as really, but spiritually, present to the faith\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} of believers in that ordinance, as the elements themselves are to their outward\index{Lord's Supper:elements:outward senses ``f10!} senses.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
29.8\ \ Although ignorant\index{ignorance ``f10!} and wicked men receive\index{Lord's Supper:wicked do not receive thing signified ``f10!} the outward elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} in this sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}: yet they receive not the thing signified thereby, but by their unworthy coming\index{Lord's Supper:unworthy participation ``f10!} thereunto are guilty\index{guilt ``f10!} of the body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!} of the Lord to their own damnation\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!}. Wherefore, all ignorant and ungodly\index{Unbelievers:ungodly ``f10!} persons, as they are unfit\index{Lord's Supper:ungodly not to be admitted ``f10!} to enjoy communion with Him, so are they unworthy of the Lord's table; and cannot, without great sin against Christ while they remain such, partake of these holy\index{Lord's Supper:elements:holy mysteries ``f10!} mysteries,\index{Lord's Supper:mystery of ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27-29, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 6:14\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  14-16, pg. ``f30!}.} or be admitted thereunto.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:6-7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}, 13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   6-7, 13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:6, 14-15\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   6, 14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 7:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 30 -- Of Church Censures} \index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!}30.1\ \ The Lord Jesus, as King\index{Jesus:King ``f10!} and Head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} of His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, has therein appointed a government, in\index{Church government:government ``f10!} the hand of Church\index{Church:institution ``f10!} officers\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!}, distinct from\index{Church government:distinct from civil ``f10!} the civil magistrate.\footnote{\ Isaiah 9:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 5:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 5:12\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:17, 28\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  17, 28, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:7\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 17, 24\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   7, 17, 24, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
30.2\ \ To these officers\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!} the keys\index{Kingdom:keys of ``f10!} of the kingdom of heaven\index{Kingdom:of heaven ``f10!} are committed: by virtue whereof, they have power\index{Church:power delegated by Christ ``f10!} respectively to retain, and remit\index{Church officers:power to retain or remit sins ``f10!} sins; to shut that kingdom against the impenitent\index{Punishment:of impenitent ``f10!}, both by the Word and\index{Scripture:word of God:standard for:life ``f10!} censures; and\index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!} to open it unto penitent\index{Repentance:penitence ``f10!} sinners, by the ministry of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, and by absolution\index{Church discipline:absolution ``f10!} from censures, as occasion shall require.\footnote{\ Matthew 16:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  16, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; John 20:21-23\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 2:6-8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
30.3\ \ Church censures are\index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!} necessary, for the reclaiming\index{Church discipline:for reclaiming offending brothers ``f10!} and gaining of offending brethren, for\index{Church discipline:for gaining offending brothers ``f10!} deterring\index{Church discipline:deterrence from sin ``f10!} of others from the like offences, for purging\index{Church discipline:purging leaven ``f10!} out of that leaven\index{leaven, spiritual ``f10!} which might infect the whole lump, for vindicating the honour of\index{Church discipline:vindicate honour of Christ ``f10!} Christ, and the holy\index{Preaching:holy profession of Gospel ``f10!} profession of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, and for preventing the wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}, which might justly fall\index{Punishment:just:on Church for failure of discipline ``f10!} upon the Church, if\index{Church:institution ``f10!} they should suffer His covenant and\index{Covenant:new:seals ``f10!} the seals\index{Sacraments:covenant seals ``f10!} thereof to be profaned by\index{Covenant:not to be profaned ``f10!} notorious\index{Church discipline:notorious offenders ``f10!} and obstinate\index{Church discipline:obstinate offenders ``f10!} offenders.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians chap. 5; 1 Timothy 5:20\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 7:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:20\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27, pg. ``f30!} to the end, with Jude 23\index{65 Jude:v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
30.4\ \ For the better attaining of these ends, the officers\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!} of the Church are\index{Church:institution ``f10!} to proceed by admonition\index{Church discipline:admonition ``f10!}; suspension\index{Church discipline:suspension from Lord's Supper ``f10!} from the sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} for a season; and\index{Lord's Supper:suspension for a season ``f10!} by excommunication\index{Church discipline:excommunication ``f10!} from the Church; according to the nature of the crime\index{Church discipline:consistent with:nature of crime ``f10!}, and demerit\index{Church discipline:consistent with:demerit of person ``f10!} of the person.\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 5:12\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:6, 14-15\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   6, 14-15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 5:4-5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}, 13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   4-5, 13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:1\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 31 -- Of Synods and Councils} \index{Church government:synods ``f10!}\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}31.1\ \ For the better government, and\index{Church government:government ``f10!} further edification of\index{Church councils:edification of Church ``f10!} the Church, there\index{Church:institution ``f10!} ought to be such assemblies\index{Church councils:assemblies to be held ``f10!} as are commonly called synods\index{Church government:synods ``f10!} or councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 15:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 4, 6\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   2, 4, 6, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
31.2\ \ As magistrates may lawfully call\index{Civil magistrate:to call synods to consult and advise ``f10!} a synod of ministers\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!}, and other fit persons, to consult and advise with, about matters of religion\index{Civil magistrate:to call synods to consult about matters of religion ``f10!};\footnote{\ Isaiah 49:23\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  49, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 19:8-11\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  19, v.   8-11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 29; 2 Chronicles 30; Matthew 2:4-5\index{40 Matthew:ch.   2, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 11:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  11, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  11, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} so, if magistrates be\index{Civil magistrate:legal authority even if:unbelievers ``f10!} open enemies\index{Enemies:of the Church ``f10!} to the Church, the\index{Church:institution ``f10!} ministers of Christ of themselves, by virtue of their office\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!}, or they, with other fit persons upon delegation\index{Church government:delegate representatives to meet with government ``f10!} from their Churches, may meet together in such assemblies\index{Church councils:assemblies to be held ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 15:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 4, 22-23, 25\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   2, 4, 22-23, 25, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the }\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription }}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Exceptions}}\textcolor{black}{).}}  
\bigskip
31.3\ \ It belongs to synods\index{Church government:synods ``f10!} and councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}, ministerially to determine controversies\index{Church councils:determine controversies of faith ``f10!} of faith and cases of conscience\index{Conscience:cases of, in controversies ``f10!}; to set down rules and\index{Church councils:set rules for public worship ``f10!} directions for the better ordering of the\index{Church councils:directions for ordering public worship ``f10!} public worship\index{Worship:public ``f10!} of God, and government of\index{Church government:government ``f10!} his Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}; to receive complaints\index{Church discipline:synods to receive complaints ``f10!} in cases of maladministration\index{Church discipline:synods to address maladministration ``f10!}, and authoritatively to determine the same: which decrees\index{Church councils:decrees ``f10!} and determinations\index{Church councils:Biblical determinations to be received ``f10!}, if consonant to the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}, are to be received with reverence and\index{Church councils:submission to ``f10!} submission; not only for their agreement with the Word, but\index{Scripture:word of God:standard:for Church ``f10!} also for the power\index{Church:power delegated by Christ ``f10!} whereby they are made, as being an ordinance of\index{Church:furnished with:ordinances of God ``f10!} God appointed thereunto in His Word.\footnote{\ Acts 15:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}, 19, 24, 27-31\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, 19, 24, 27-31, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:4\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17-20, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
31.4\ \ All synods\index{Church government:synods ``f10!} or councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}, since the Apostles\index{Apostles:apostles ``f10!}{}' times, whether general or particular, may err\index{Church councils:may err ``f10!}; and many have erred\index{Church councils:many have erred ``f10!}. Therefore they are not to be made the rule of faith\index{Faith:rule of ``f10!}, or practice; but to be used as a help in\index{Church councils:not the rule of faith or practice, but help ``f10!} both.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:24\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
31.5\ \ Synods\index{Church government:synods ``f10!} and councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!} are to handle, or conclude, nothing, but that which is ecclesiastical\index{Church councils:to address only ecclesiastical matters ``f10!}: and are not to intermeddle with civil affairs which\index{Church councils:not to meddle with civil affairs ``f10!} concern the commonwealth\index{commonwealth ``f10!}; unless by way of humble\index{Church councils:to receive humble petitions ``f10!} petition, in cases extraordinary; or by way of advice, for satisfaction of conscience, if\index{Conscience:satisfaction of ``f10!} they be thereunto required by the civil\index{Civil magistrate:to call synods to consult and advise ``f10!} magistrate.\footnote{\ Luke 12:13-14\index{42 Luke:ch.  12, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; John 18:36\index{43 John:ch.  18, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 32 -- Of the State of Man After Death, and of the Resurrection of the Dead} \index{Death:following:state of man ``f10!}\index{Resurrection:general, of dead ``f10!}32.1\ \ The bodies of men, after death\index{Death:bodies:return to dust ``f10!}, return to dust\index{Adam:formed of dust ``f10!} and see corruption:\index{Death:corruption of body ``f10!}\footnote{\ Genesis 3:19\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:3\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}6\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} but their souls (which neither die nor\index{Mankind:immortal soul ``f10!} sleep) having an immortal subsistence, immediately return to God who gave them:\index{Believers:souls made perfect at death ``f10!}\footnote{\ Luke 23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 12:7\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} the souls of the righteous, being then\index{Resurrection:believers:perfected ``f10!} made perfect in holiness\index{Believers:holy:made perfect at death ``f10!}, are received into the highest heavens, where\index{Heaven:God's abode ``f10!} they behold\index{Believers:behold face of God in glory ``f10!} the face of\index{Resurrection:believers:behold face of God ``f10!} God, in light and glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:light ``f10!}, waiting for\index{Resurrection:believers:waiting expectantly ``f10!} the full redemption\index{Redemption:full ``f10!} of their bodies.\index{Bodies in graves:believers ``f10!}\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 5:1, 6, 8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, 6, 8, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 1:23\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!} with Acts 3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!} and Ephesians 4:10\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} And the souls of the wicked are\index{Judgement day:wicked:cast into:hell ``f10!} cast into\index{Punishment:hell:wicked cast into ``f10!} hell\index{Hell:hell ``f10!}, where they remain in torments and\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} utter darkness\index{darkness, spiritual ``f10!}, reserved to the judgment of the\index{Judgement:final ``f10!} great day.\footnote{\ Luke 16:23-24\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 1:25\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 6\index{65 Jude:v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{65 Jude:v. 6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Peter 3:19.} Beside these two places, for soul\index{Superiors:to:provide inferiors with things necessary for soul and body ``f10!}s separated\index{Death:soul separated from body ``f10!} from their bodies, the\index{Bodies in graves:believers and unbelievers ``f10!} Scripture acknowledges\index{Last day:heaven or hell, no other option ``f10!} none.   
\bigskip
