32.2\ \ At the last day\index{Last day:last day ``f10!}, such as are found alive\index{Last day:those alive on earth ``f10!} shall not die, but\index{Last day:not all shall die ``f10!} be changed:\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 4:17\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:51-52\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  51-52, pg. ``f30!}.} and all the dead\index{Death:following:all men raised ``f10!} shall be raised up, with the selfsame bodies, and none other, although with different qualities\index{Resurrection:bodies:different qualities ``f10!}, which shall be united again\index{Resurrection:bodies:united to souls ``f10!} to their souls for ever.\footnote{\ Job 19:26-27\index{18 Job:ch.  19, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}2-44\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  42-44, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
32.3\ \ The bodies of the\index{Resurrection:bodies:same ones as before death, for just and unjust ``f10!} unjust shall, by the power\index{Resurrection:believers:by the power of Christ ``f10!} of Christ, be raised to dishonour\index{Resurrection:wicked raised in dishonour ``f10!}: the bodies of the just, by His Spirit, unto\index{Holy Spirit:raises bodies of just to honour ``f10!} honour; and\index{Resurrection:believers:raised in honour ``f10!} be made conformable\index{Resurrection:bodies:conformable to Christ's ``f10!} to His own glorious body\index{Jesus:resurrection:body:glorious ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 24:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  24, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:28-29\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:21\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}  

\section{Chapter 33 -- Of the Last Judgment} \index{Judgement:final ``f10!}33.1\ \ God has appointed a day, wherein He will judge the\index{Jesus:judge:world ``f10!} world in righteousness\index{Judgement day:in righteousness ``f10!}, by Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} to whom all power\index{Jesus:almighty power ``f10!} and judgment is given\index{Jesus:judge:assigned by Father ``f10!} of the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 5:22, 27\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  22, 27, pg. ``f30!}.} In which day, not only the apostate angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} shall be judged\index{Angels:apostate, to be judged ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 6:3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 6\index{65 Jude:v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 2:4\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} but likewise all persons that have lived upon earth shall appear before the tribunal\index{Judgement day:tribunal of Christ ``f10!} of Christ, to give an account of their thoughts, words, and deeds\index{Judgement day:account for thoughts, words, and deeds ``f10!}; and to receive according to what they have done in the body, whether good or evil\index{Judgement day:give account of deeds, whether good or evil ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:10\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 12:1\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 14:10, 12\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:36\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}{}-37\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  36-37, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
33.2\ \ The end of God's appointing this day is for the manifestation of the glory of His\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} mercy, in\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} the eternal salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} of the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}; and of His justice\index{God's attributes:administers justice ``f10!}, in the damnation\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!} of the reprobate\index{Punishment:of reprobate ``f10!} who are wicked and\index{Judgement day:wicked:damned ``f10!} disobedient\index{Judgement day:disobedient cast into hell ``f10!}. For then shall the righteous go\index{Resurrection:believers:to everlasting life ``f10!} into everlasting life\index{everlasting life ``f10!}, and receive that fulness of joy\index{Joy:everlasting ``f10!} and refreshing\index{Judgement day:believers:joy and refreshing ``f10!}, which shall come from the presence of the Lord: but the wicked who\index{Judgement day:wicked:cast into:eternal torments ``f10!} know not God, and obey not\index{Punishment:those who do not obey the Gospel ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} of Jesus Christ, shall be cast into\index{Punishment:hell:wicked cast into ``f10!} eternal torments, and\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} be punished with everlasting destruction from\index{Punishment:everlasting:destruction ``f10!} the presence of the Lord, and from the glory of His power.\footnote{\ Matthew 25:31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  31, pg. ``f30!} to the end, Romans 2:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:22-23\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 3:19\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 1:7\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   7-10, pg. ``f30!}.}   
\bigskip
33.3\ \ As Christ would have us to be certainly persuaded that\index{Judgement day:be persuaded that there is ``f10!} there shall be a day of judgment\index{Judgement day:believers:perfected ``f10!}, both to deter\index{Judgement day:knowledge as deterrence from sin ``f10!} all men from sin, and for the greater consolation of the godly in their adversity\index{Judgement day:encourage godly in adversity ``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Peter 3:11, 14\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.  11, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 5:10\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 1:5-7\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   5-7, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 21:27-28\index{42 Luke:ch.  21, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  23-25, pg. ``f30!}.} so will He have that day unknown\index{Judgement day:day unknown to men ``f10!} to men, that they may shake off all carnal security\index{Idolatry:carnal:security ``f10!}, and be always watchful, because\index{Jesus:return:watchfulness ``f10!} they know not at what hour the\index{Jesus:return:no one knows hour ``f10!} Lord will come; and may be ever prepared\index{Last day:be prepared to say, 'Come, Lord Jesus' ``f10!} to say, Come, Lord Jesus, come quickly, Amen\index{Amen, testimony of our true desire for God's glory ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 24:36\index{40 Matthew:ch.  24, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}, 42-44\index{40 Matthew:ch.  24, v.  36, 42-44, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 13:35-37\index{41 Mark:ch.  13, v.  35-37, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 12:35-36\index{42 Luke:ch.  12, v.  35-36, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}
